##### 3.2.5.1.2 PRACH Mapping with SS/PBCH blocks

###### 3.2.5.1.2.0-1 PRACH Mapping with SS/PBCH blocks Algorithm PRACH Mapping with SS/PBCH blocks (ID: 11111961)

**3.2.5.1.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `13480955`)

PRACH Mapping with SS/PBCH blocks If NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion is “one”:

 Each configured SS/PBCH block (see definition in 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is mapped to one PRACH occasion per mapping cycle and there is at least one mapping cycle per PRACH association period. ith configured SSB **is associated to rrmPrachOccasionIndex equal to i+j *Number Of configured SSBs, with j in range of [0.. floor(rrmNbPrachOccassionInPrachAssociationPeriod / Number Of configured SSB)-1].**

 All RA preambles within range [0..cbraPreamblesPerSsb-1] received in each PRACH occasion are CBRA preambles allocated to the mapped SSB.

 All RA preambles within range [cbraPreamblesPerSsb..totalNumberOfRAPreambles-1] received in each PRACH occasion are CFRA preambles allocated to the mapped SSB.

 rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP = floor(rrmNbPrachOccassionInPrachAssociationPeriod / nConfiguredSsPbch) * nConfiguredSsPbch, is the number of valid ROs in a PRACH Association Period. 

If NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion is “two” or “four”:

1\. The algorithm to determine valid RACH occasion (RO). A valid RO in a PRACH Association Period (5G_UP_ALG_1962_replaced([11111925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRIPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is with rrmPrachOccasionIndex = i_valid, where i_valid in range of [0.. rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP-1].

 rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP = ceiling(rrmNbMappingCyclesInPrachAP * rrmNbRoPerCycle), is the number of valid ROs in a PRACH Association Period.

where:

 rrmNbMappingCyclesInPrachAP = floor(rrmNbPrachOccassionInPrachAssociationPeriod * nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion / nConfiguredSsPbch), is the max integer number of SSB to ROs mapping cycles within an PRACH association period,

 rrmNbRoPerCycle = nConfiguredSsPbch / nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion, is the number of ROs required for each cycle of mapping SSBs to ROs.

  1. The algorithm to build RO and SSB list association. For each valid RO, the associated SSB list = {inth configured SSB}.



 in = (rrmPrachOccasionIndex * nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion + **n) mod nConfiguredSsPbch,**

 If the RO is not the last valid RO (rrmPrachOccasionIndex < rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP-1), then **n is in range of [0..nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion-1].**

 If the RO is the last valid RO (rrmPrachOccasionIndex = rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP-1), then **n is in range of [0..stop], where istop = nConfiguredSsPbch-1.**

3\. The algorithm to derive (SSB, CBRA or CFRA) from (rrmPrachOccasionIndex, preamble index) upon receive a PRACH preamble.

a) To derive Msg1 SSB from (rrmPrachOccasionIndex, preamble index):

 NumberOfRAPreamblesPerSsb = totalNumberOfRAPreambles / nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion, is the number of preambles associated with a SSB,

 **n = floor(preamble index / NumberOfRAPreamblesPerSsb), is the index applied on the associated SSB list for the RO indexed by rrmPrachOccasionIndex. It represents the preamble index belongs to the** nth SSB of the associated SSB list.****

 **i** n = (rrmPrachOccasionIndex * nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion + **n) mod nConfiguredSsPbch.** ****

 The **i** nth configured SSB (see definition in 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is the derived SSB.****

b) To derive CBRA or CFRA from the preamble index:

 If the preamble index < (**n * NumberOfRAPreamblesPerSsb+ cbraPreamblesPerSsb), then it is CBRA, else it is CFRA.**

Notes:

 For the determined SSB,

o pstart = **n * NumberOfRAPreamblesPerSsb,**

o pstop_cbra = pstart + cbraPreamblesPerSsb - 1,

o pstart_cfra = pstop_cbra + 1,

o pstop = pstart + NumberOfRAPreamblesPerSsb - 1,

o CBRA preambles in range of [pstart .. pstop_cbra],

o CFRA preambles in range of [pstart_cfra .. pstop].

 5G_UP_ALG_28176_replaced([11106057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koTe5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ensures the preamble index is in valid range so that this algorithm need not to check:

o the validity of preamble index,

o whether or not the RO indexed by rrmPrachOccasionIndex is the last RO in the PRACH association period.

Where:

 nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion: the number of SSBs that can be mapped to one RO. It is derived from NIDD parameter NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion. “one” is 1, “two” is 2, “four” is 4.

 totalNumberOfRAPreambles: NIDD parameter NRCELL-totalNumberOfRAPreambles.

 cbraPreamblesPerSsb: derived from NIDD parameter NRCELL-cbraPreamblesPerSsb, n4 is 4, n8 is 8, and so on.

 nConfiguredSsPbch: Number of configured SSB, refer 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 rrmPrachOccasionIndex: RO index within a PRACH Association Period, refer 5G_UP_ALG_1965_replaced([11111936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRvQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 rrmNbPrachOccassionInPrachAssociationPeriod refer 5G_UP_ALG_1962_replaced([11111925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRIPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The configured SSB list: see definition in 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1\. Refer TS 38.213 8.1 for rationale of this requirement.

2\. FDD supports only nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion is 1.

3\. The method for "two" and "four" is generic and applicable for "one". Considering the method "one" is less CPU cost, so the requirement keeps as is.

If the cell is not FR1 Supplementary Downlink only (SDL)(5G_UP_ALG_1802_replaced([11110656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGwJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and not in conformance test mode, gNB shall calculate rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP as above.

If the cell is FR1 Supplementary Donwlink only (SDL) or in conformance test mode, then rrmNbValidRoInPrachAP is not relevant.

**[Before CB013712-B]** In FR2, if the SS/PBCH block is inactive (see definition for active or inactive SS/PBCH [11347149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa4fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), the PRACH occasion computation continues (the bit concerned by the inactive SS/PBCH is 0), the PRACH occasion is not used and not requested to L1.[End **CB013712-B]**

---

#### 3.2.5.1.3 PRACH configuration error handling

##### 3.2.5.1.3.0-1 PRACH configuration error handling Status and diagnostic information report (ID: 11111984)

**3.2.5.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11111988`)

PRACH configuration error handling When the gNB is not able to find enough valid PRACH occasions within the PRACH association for the configured SS/PBCH (see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the cell setup procedure is rejected with the followiing data.

By default all diagnosticInformation[0-13] fields are initialized to 0x00000000 and when the check is failed, then the gNB reports a negative acknowledgement with the following information:

 The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G_NotOk).

 The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G_InvalidParameter).

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is filled with the value 0x00000007.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is set to the value of prachConfigurationIndex.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is set to the number of PRACH in frequency domain (0: ”one” ; 1: ”two” ; 2: ”four” ; 3: ”eight”).

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set to the number of SS/PBCH per PRACH occasion (0: ”oneEighth” ; 1: ”oneFourth” ; 2: ”oneHalf” ; 3: ”one” ; 4: ”two” ; 5: ”four” ; 6: ”eight” ; 7: ”sixteen”).

 The “diagnosticInformation[4-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.2.5.1.3.0-2 PRACH configuration error handling Additional alarm information (ID: 11111993)

**3.2.5.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11111996`)

PRACH configuration error handling The additional text sent in the alarm by the gNB is detailed hereafter, when faultId is set to EFaultId_GnbCpRtCellUpdateFailedAl with the extraFaultInfo[0] set to 0x00000007.

Cause: Invalid PRACH configuration (not enough valid PRACH occasions to map the configured SS/PBCH within a PRACH association).

PRACH configuration index : 

number of PRACH in frequency domain : < extraFaultInfo[2]=0, ”one” ; extraFaultInfo[2]=1, ”two” ; extraFaultInfo[2]=2, ”four” ; extraFaultInfo[2]=3, ”eight” >

number of SS/PBCH per PRACH occasion: < extraFaultInfo[3]=0, ”oneEighth” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=1, ”oneFourth” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=2, ”oneHalf” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=3, ”one” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=4, ”two” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=5, ”four” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=6, ”eight” ; extraFaultInfo[3]=7, ”sixteen” >

---

## 3.2.6 Beam Tracking and Beam Refinement

### 3.2.6.1 Beam Management Type

#### 3.2.6.1.0-1 Beam Management Type Beam Management Type Modes (ID: 11112007)

**3.2.6.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11112012`)

Beam Management Type Beam Management shall be UE specifically conducted according to the value of appliedBeamRefinementP2 in PsUser_UserSetupReq > CellConfigParam structure [5G_CP_ARC_ALG_774_replaced([11242191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tmv24fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

5G-L2-PS shall support the update of appliedBeamRefinementP2 during UE reconfiguration procedure. 

Note: Possible scenrios for update of appliedBeamRefinementP2 :

  * Due to maxNumberCSI-RS-Resource across all CCs for refine beam support may exceed UE capability, gNB will trigger UE reconfiguration from CSI-RS RSRP report to SSB RSRP report together with Scell addition. Once the reconfiguration happens, 5G-L2-PS need to consider the transient period for PCell beam report. At the same time, the reconfiguration from SSB RSRP report to CSI-RS RSRP report due to Scell release will also need 5G-L2-PS to consider the transient period for PCell beam report, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2687_replaced([11120600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for handling of Scell release.

---

#### 3.2.6.1.0-2 Beam Management Type Beam Tracking and Beam Refinement for Digital Beamforming with Carrier Aggregation (ID: 11112015)

**3.2.6.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11112031`)

Beam Management Type Additionally to the configuration of Beam Tracking and Beam Refinement on PSCell, if UEs are configured with SCell, following configuration is set up and conducted in SCell. For digital beamforming (rrmBeamformingType =digitalBf, 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), a beam tracking and beam refinement process (if nrBtsBeamRefinementP2=true) shall be separately set up and conducted in SCell as defined by 5GC000533-B/C/D via parameters during cell setup. A different beam can be reported and used for each component carrier (PSCell and SCell). For SCell a CSI measurement configuration shall be used (as defined in 5G_L3_FLOW_7776). Beam reports, see 5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), of an SCell shall be received via PSCell.

For FR1 TDD Scell with supercell mode enabled or BF activated, 5G-L2-PS shall mark the Scell target beam ID as invalid just after Scell activation according to 5G_UP_ALG_2703_replaced([11120833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqURHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for blind Scell activation and 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for buffer-based Scell activation. 5G-L2-PS shall update the Scell target beam ID to UE context according to 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) once Scell beam report is received according to 5G_UP_ALG_3617_replaced([11160013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For FR1 TDD SCell with UL CA configured and supercell mode enabled [CB009543-C1] or a TDD supercell SCell with an FDD supercell PCell [End CB009543-C1], the SCell target beam ID is not selected based on SCell beam report, see 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the SCell target beam ID update.

---

#### 3.2.6.1.0-3 Beam Management Type Beam Tracking for Analog Beamforming with Carrier Aggregation (ID: 11112034)

**3.2.6.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13476971`)

Beam Management Type If Carrier Aggregation feature is activated and UEs are configured with one or more SCells, for analog beamforming (rrmBeamformingType = analogBf, 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), beam reporting shall be conducted only on PSCell of a UE as defined in 5GC000535-D. Beam reporting is not configured for SCells. Same beam as used (selected) in the PSCell is applied also for all the SCells of a UE.

---

#### 3.2.6.1.0-4 Beam Management Type PMI beam usage for TDD (ID: 11112043)

**3.2.6.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13136348`)

Beam Management Type [Before CNI-137616-C] Use R&D parameter rdDisableBestPmiBeamForPdcch [5G_UP_ALG_8458_replaced([11113959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] to control the beam for PDCCH when dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and dlEcpriFdBeamforming is true. The default R&D parameter value shall be 1. [End CNI-137616-C]

If [Before CNI-137616-C] (R&D parameter(rdDisableBestPmiBeamForPdcch ) is 1) and [End CNI-137616-C] (dlEcpriFdBeamforming is true)

PMI beam pattern Id shall be computed from CSI feedback to select beam used for UE's PDSCH at least.

if dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false **Refer to ([11113014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

if dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true,

refer to ([11113316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UE report based best SSB beam is used for PDCCH transmission.

Else

The PMI beam pattern Id shall be computed from CSI feedback to select beam used for UE's PDSCH**, PDCCH at least.**

if dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false **Refer to ([11113014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

if dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true, refer to ([11113316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End

Note: CL 8x4 MIMO must have actBeamforming be set as true and numofSubsecotor is 0.

Note: CL 8x4 MIMO only works with TDD FR1, Dl C4 subcell.

---

#### 3.2.6.1.0-5 Beam Management Type PMI beam usage for FDD (ID: 12763343)

**3.2.6.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12763286`)

Beam Management Type If the cell is has FDD BF enable and dlMimoMode is CL 32x4, PMI beams can be used according to [11112298: Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

PMI beam shall be computed from CSI report for channel acquisition based on 8 ports and 32 ports CSI-RS according to: [11112756: PatternIDs for PMI beams](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZECvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11112962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

---

### 3.2.6.2 Beam Measurement for Beam change

#### 3.2.6.2.1 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change

#### 3.2.6.2.1-1 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change

##### 3.2.6.2.1-1.0-1 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change When a beamformingMeasurementMetric is received as defined in [5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced( 11112073 )], the power values of each beam ID shall be filtered. Beam reporting case: Reported power value of best beam shall be converted to power value by formula absolute_value = -157dBm + reported_value, see [3GPP 38.133, table 10.1.6.1-1]. Relative power values shall be converted to absolute values before filtering by formula absolute_value = (reference_value - reported_value * 2) dBm. If relative value = 'out of range', then absolute_value = max( (reference_value - 30dB), -140) dBm. NOTE: According to beam reporting as defined in 3GPP TS 38.214, reported L1-RSRP values (that is a power value example) are defined by a 7-bit value in the range [-140, -44] dBm with 1dB step size. The relative L1-RSRP uses a 4-bit value, with 2dB step. Relative RSRP value 0b1111 shall be considered as 'out of range' special value. It means that the difference is bigger than 30dB. Filtering Per beam ID, the (infinite impulse response (IIR)) filtering of power values is defined by: y_dBm(k) = rdBeamMgmtPowerFilterCoefficient y_dBm(k-1) + (1 - rdBeamMgmtPowerFilterCoefficient) x_dBm(k), with 0&lt; rdBeamMgmtPowerFilterCoefficient&lt;1, where y is the filtered power value in [dBm], x is the reported or measured power value [dBm], rdBeamMgmtPowerFilterCoefficient defined in [5G_L2_3724_replaced( 11183458 )], and k is the current time. If unknown beam ID is measured, empty filter shall be used or, if all filters are used, the filter with oldest measured value shall be overwritten. NOTE: the source beam filter must not be overwritten since needed in [5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced( 11112105 )]. If a filtered beam ID = i is not reported, update the filtered power value assuming x_dBm(k) = min((filtered value of beam ID = i), (measured value of weakest beam - 2 dB)) in above formular. The number of filters is defined by the parameter rdNumBeamMgmtPowerFilter as defined in [5G_L2_3726_replaced( 11183479 )]. (ID: 11112101)

#### 3.2.6.2.1-2 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change

##### 3.2.6.2.1-2.0-1 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change A given beam ID = i shall only be a target beam for the next beam change, if the filtered power value of beam ID = i is larger than the source beam value by an offset value defined by the parameter rdBeamMgmtPowerOffset_dB as defined in [5G_L2_3725_replaced( 11183468 )]. That is if this condition is met: filteredReceivePower_dBm[beam ID = i] &gt; filteredReceivePower_dBm[source beam] +  rdBeamMgmtPowerOffset_dB. NOTE: Linked to both 5GC000533 and 5GC000535 features to avoid creating a dependency on their mutual implementation order. NOTE: the beam selection is impacted if appliedUlBeamSweeping = TRUE, if appliedUlBeamFallback = TRUE, or if appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange= TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced( 11111451 )). (ID: 11112108)

#### 3.2.6.2.1-3 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change

##### 3.2.6.2.1-3.0-1 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change If for a given user two beams are measured, in [5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced( 11112105 )], "source beam" can be 1st or 2nd measured beam in the equation filteredReceivePower_dBm[beam ID = i] &gt; filteredReceivePower_dBm[source beam] +  rdBeamMgmtPowerOffset_dB. NOTE: In 5G19 the dlMimoMode "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO", as defined in NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode, can be used to anticipate measuring or reporting of a second beam. (ID: 11112117)

#### 3.2.6.2.1-4 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change

##### 3.2.6.2.1-4.0-3 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change 12798809: BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change 12798809: BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change 12798809: Beam change 12798809: BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change 12798809: BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change 12798809: BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change [Before CNI-137616-B] CRI based second beam selection shall be conducted and follow the rules in this requirement when R&amp;D parameter rdOrthogonalBeamsForceCRI =1. After 1st target beam is selected with highest filtered value filteredReceivePower_dBm[beam ID = i] (Please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced( 11112105 )), 2nd target beam shall be selected according to below rules: 1. Compare all available beams in the UE context (Note2, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1999_replaced( 11112098 )), find all beam candidates for 2nd target beam except 1st target beam if filteredReceivePower_dBm[beam ID = i] &gt; filteredReceivePower_dBm[1st target beam] - rdRsrpRssiOffsetLimit. 2. Select 2nd target beam from all the beam candidates in step 1 if it has highest received power filteredReceivePower_dBm[beam ID = i] and  is not a neighbour beam of the 1st target beam. The neighbour beam of the 1st target beam is defined by the CRI value below [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a table with two columns and five rows. The first column is labeled "1stCRI %4" and the second column is labeled "2ndCRI-1stCRI". The rows contain numerical data. 1stCRI %4 2ndCRI-1stCRI 0 (-3,-1,1,2,3) 1 (-1,1,2,3,5) 2 (-5,-3,-3,-1,1) 3 (-3,-2,-1,1,3) 3. If no beam is found in step 1, force to use 1st target beam ID-1 as new 2nd target beam if CRI of 1st target beam larger than CRI of 2nd target beam; force to use 1st target beam ID +1 as new 2nd target beam if CRI of 1st target beam equal to or smaller than CRI of 2nd target beam. 4. Set filteredReceivePower_dBm[2st target beam] to max power level so that the 2nd target beam can be selected as final 2nd target beam in 5G_UP_ALG_2010_replaced( 11112113 ). The second beam selection in PR530808 shall be supported only for one SSB beam row beam set (Note 5). 6. rdOrthogonalBeamsForceCRI is a new R&amp;D parameter which is introduced to active CRI based second beam selection, it is specified in 5G_L2_1384_replaced( 11183719 ), the default value is 0(disabled). 7. rdReceivePowerOffsetLimit_dB is the received power offset limitation for 2nd target beam which is specified in 5G_L2_1383_replaced( 11183713 ). Note1: rdOrthogonalBeamsForceCRI can be set to 1 only if appliedBeamRefinementP2 is set to “true”.** Note2: Available beams are controlled by rdNumBeamMgmtRsrpFilter(default 4) and reported timing(note3) in case of CRI based refine beam. rdNumBeamMgmtRsrpFilter shall be changed to a larger value which is not exceed the value of 4 nActivatedSsPbch (see 5G_UP_82_replaced( 11347116 )) , such as 8/16 if rdOrthogonalBeamsForceCRI is set to 1 *** Note3: power is RSRP in case of CRI based. Note4: With time goes on, receive power of not reported beams will be reduced by 1dBm every beam report. If unknown beam ID is reported, empty filter shall be used or, if all filters are used, the filter with oldest reported value shall be overwritten. The source beam filter must not be overwritten since needed in 5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced( 11112105 ). Please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1999_replaced( 11112098 ) Note5: This algorithm is not applicable for beam sets of two to four SSB rows which is specified in 5G_UP_ALG_1933_replaced( 11111686 ). Please see the example below: [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a table with 5 rows and 9 columns. The first column contains the labels "SSB beamld", "CRI", and "refined beamld". The remaining 8 columns are labeled "SSB0" through "SSB7". The cells within the table contain numerical data. The cell at the intersection of "SSB2" and "CRI" row, and "SSB3" column is highlighted in yellow. SSB beamld SSB0 SSB1 SSB2 SSB3 SSB4 SSB5 SSB6 SSB7 CRI 0 1 4 5 8 9 12 13 2 3 6 7 10 11 14 15 refined beamld 8 16 9 17 10 18 11 19 24 32 25 33 26 34 27 35 For example in above table, if the 1st target beam Id is 11, with 1st CRI=12, CRI= {9/11/13/14/15} are neighbour beams because CRI 9/11/13/14/15-1st CRI(12)= -3/-1/1/2/3. [End CNI-137616-B] Note: CRI based second beam selection is removed by CNI-137616 due to R&amp;D parameter removal. (ID: 12798809)

#### 3.2.6.2.1-5 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change

##### 3.2.6.2.1-5.0-3 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change If NRBTS/NRCELL/beamSet.tiltOffset / leftEdgeAngle / rightEdgeAngle / basicBeamSet [CB014301-C] / customBeamSetName [End CB014301-C] is/are  online changed by operator, SSB/refined beam set are online changed accordingly. When L2-PS receives the notification of SSB/refined beam set online changed, L2-PS shall start to use the new beam set instead of the old one. For each UE, L2-PS shall initialize the measurement beamformingmeasurementMetric of each beam. When L2-PS receives the first valid beam report (the DTX beam reports received on PUCCH format 2 or format 3 shall be discarded) after the notification, L2-PS shall select the target beam from the beam report as:**** The beam with highest L1-RSRP in beam report is the target beam. If two target beams are required, then the beams with highest and second highest L1-RSRP in beam report are the two target beams. If there is only one beam in the beam report, then the second target beam is the random neighbour beam of the first target beam (note: following the same method in RACH). Before L2 receives the first valid beam report, L2-PS shall use the current target beams in UE context. L2-PS shall update target beam ID in UE context as 11112151 . L2-PS shall apply the target beam to physical channels as 11112294 . After the first valid beam report, the target beam selection method is same as 11112105 / 11112113 . (ID: 12775764)

##### 3.2.6.2.1.0-1 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change Purpose (ID: 11112059)

**3.2.6.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11112070`)

BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change The beamformingMeasurementMetric [5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] value(s) shall define the target beam(s) which shall be considered in [5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

The beamformingMeasurementMetric applies also to supercell configuration where the target beam considered is the target SSB beam. For FR1 TDD SCell with UL CA configured and supercell mode enabled [CB009543-C1] or a TDD supercell SCell with an FDD supercell PCell [End CB009543-C1], the SCell target beam is not selected based on SCell beam report, and see 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the SCell target beam ID update.

NOTE:

  * if beam refinement is switched on controlled by appliedBeamRefinementP2 (5G_UP_ALG_1974_replaced([11112003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpSWUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), beamformingPowerMetric is measured on CSI-RS for beam refinement, i.e., CRI is reported, otherwise L1 RSRP measurement is based on SSB beams, i.e., SSBRI is reported. Which value to report is indicated to the UE via RRC message, see 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2263_replaced([11334666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wVIptPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and IEs mentioned there.
  * CRI reports will be available only with this subfeature.



NOTE: Linked to both 5GC000533 and 5GC000535 features to avoid creating a dependency on their mutual implementation order.

---

##### 3.2.6.2.1.0-2 BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change beamformingMeasurementMetric (ID: 11112073)

**3.2.6.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11112078`)

BeamformingMeasurementMetric for Beam change The beamformingMeasurementMetric defines per measured beam a value for the beam ID and corresponding power value in dBm.

When a UCI beam report is received via Format 2 or Format 3 as defined in [5G_UP_ALG_3617_replaced([11160013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))], and if the report quantity = "CRI-RSRP" or = "SSBRI-RSRP" [3GPP TS 38.214], the received RSRP values of each beam ID shall be used. The corresponding reported CRI or SSBRI value(s) shall be the target beam(s) in the UE context according to [5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

NOTE: According to beam reporting as defined in 3GPP TS 38.214, reported L1-RSRP values (that is a power value example) are defined by a 7-bit value in the range [-140, -44] dBm with 1dB step size. The relative L1-RSRP uses a 4-bit value, with 2dB step.

Relative RSRP value 0b1111 shall be considered as 'out of range' special value. It means that the difference is bigger than 30dB.

5G-L2-PS shall discard DTX'ed beam reports received via Format 2 or Format 3. If a beam report is nonDTX'ed and has an instantaneous SINR value (5G_UP_ALG_3623_replaced([11160031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) <rdThresholdUciBm_dB (5G_L2_1247_replaced([11191901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28gZlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and report payload received over Format 3 is less than 20bit (6bit CRC length) and UCI does not arrive over PUSCH 5G-L2-PS must not take reported CRI or SSBRI value(s) as target beam. Only if the next UCI for beam report is nonDTX'ed and includes the same CRI or SSBRI value(s) as the one before, 5G-L2-PS shall take confirmed CRI or SSBRI value(s) as the target beam(s), see 5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwise if instantaneous SINR value of the beam report is < rdThresholdUciBm_dB (5G_L2_1247_replaced([11191901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28gZlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS must not consider a new target beam and must not change the beam. If there is no target beam Id in UE context for CA UE over Scell scheduler, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the beam report with dtxMeasurements.dtx == nonDTX as valid target beam and update target beam to UE context according to 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and don't check the instantaneous SINR according to 5G_UP_ALG_3623_replaced([11160031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 3.2.6.3 Update Target Beam ID in UE Context

#### 3.2.6.3.0-1 Update Target Beam ID in UE Context Update SSB/Refined Beam ID in UE Context (ID: 11112156)

**3.2.6.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11112167`)

Update Target Beam ID in UE Context If the target beam for the next beam change is selected according to 5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced([11112105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or in 5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the beam ID shall be stored in the UE context to be available for retrieving the related pattern ID.

NOTE: beam Id in RACH procedure as in 5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actSupercell = True and for a given user two beams are reported, reported 2nd best beam measurement is used for metric calculation; 2nd best beam is not selected. Otherwise, if MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actSupercell = False, then

If for a given user two beams are reported, the 2nd beam ID shall be stored in the user context.

For FR1 TDD SCell with UL CA configured and supercell mode enabled [CB009543-C1] or a TDD supercell SCell with an FDD supercell PCell [End CB009543-C1], the SCell target beam ID shall be updated and stored in the UE context when SCell is activated or subcell is switched on PCell, and the beam ID mapped to the subcell which is collocated and overlaid with the serving subcell on PCell shall be selected as the target beam ID on SCell (see 5G_UP_5553_replaced([11353464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hXvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB009543-C1]

In a similar fashion, for FR1 a FDD SCell with supercell mode enabled, the SCell serving subcell ID shall be updated and stored in the UE context when SCell is activated or subcell is switched on PCell. The subcell ID which is collocated and overlaid with the serving subcell on PCell shall be selected as the serving subcell ID on the SCell (see 5G_UP_ALG_28461_replaced([11113896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfKqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB009543-C1]

NOTE: the beam selection is impacted if appliedUlBeamSweeping = TRUE, if appliedUlBeamFallback = TRUE, or if appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange= TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE: Beam ID can be related to an SSB beam or a refined beam or in case of supercell, beam ID refers to the virtual SSB beam associated with L1 subcell.

NOTE: Linked to both 5GC000533 and 5GC000535 features to avoid creating a dependency on their mutual implementation order.

NOTE: signaling of beam change and using new beam remains as defined by 5GC000533-B or -C and [5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

NOTE: In 5G19 the dlMimoMode "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO", as defined in NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode, can be used to anticipate reporting or measuring of a second beam.

---

### 3.2.6.4 Two or more beams for SUMIMO

#### 3.2.6.4.1 Two beams for DL SUMIMO

#### 3.2.6.4.1-1 Two beams for DL SUMIMO

##### 3.2.6.4.1-1.0-1 Two beams for DL SUMIMO Co-existence of different beam types for one UE or one cell for DL (ID: 11112244)

**3.2.6.4.1-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11112249`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true 5G-L2-PS shall apply the DL beams for the same UE in following order, if the beam type is available and preferred per channel and reference signal:

  1. SRS based Sub-band beams (5G_UP_ALG_13891_replaced([11112241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UEs with Subband beamforming enabled (5G_UP_ALG_21269_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

  2. SRS based oDFT beams (5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UEs that has sub-band SRS state machine running as 5G_UP_ALG_6962_replaced([11155660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), or 5G_UP_ALG_2135_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));




3.[CB008322-E] PMI beams (5G_UP_ALG_2028_replaced([11112211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if NRCELL/dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 and the UE has 8 port CSI-RS configured; [End CB008322-E]

  1. Otherwise SSB/refined beams (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



Note: refer to NIDD parameter relation, actDlSrsSubbandBm is true must have actDlSrsBm as true, actBeamforming as true, dlMimoMode as CL 8x4 or CL 4x4 or OL 4x4.

---

##### 3.2.6.4.1-1.0-2 Two beams for DL SUMIMO Four beams from SRS for PDSCH (ID: 11112252)

**3.2.6.4.1-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11112263`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO [Before CB008322-A]If short-term beamforming is enabled (5G_UP_5798_replaced([11354249](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucGPDvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

  * If subband BWVs are valid (5G_UP_ALG_13875_replaced([11156746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3Ow_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),



Denote number of subband BWVs received from L1 as N.

Decide rank that would be used by PDSCH as below:

If rdRankForRtBeam (5G_UP_ALG_19887_replaced([11158576](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktDcA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0:

If the rank that is adjusted by L2 (5G_UP_ALG_3210_replaced([11139690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpGx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or transient phase), then this adjusted rank would be used; else if N would be used.

else if rdRankForRtBeam is 1: Always rank decided by L2 will be used.

else: none

If the rank decided is the same as N, then PDSCH scheduling of this UE shall adopt rank N with subband beams.

Else: L2 shall apply PMI/SSB/refined beam (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UE’s PDSCH scheduling.

  * Else: L2 shall apply PMI/SSB/refined beam (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UE’s PDSCH scheduling.



For retransmission of PDSCH, if the latest subband BWVs have relevant rank different than the rank of retransmission, then legacy PMI/SSB/refined beam would be used.

PMI beam shall only be used when they are valid. For UEs those are not configured with 8 ports-CSI-RS, PMI beams are always invalid.

For UEs under 8 ports or 32 ports mode, when legacy beam is used, port selection (5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for PDSCH rank 2 shall always be adopted. 

[End CB008322-A]

[CB008322-A] If the UE is subband beamforming enabled UE (5G_UP_ALG_21269_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

  * If all the criteria for subband BWVs usage defined in 5G_UP_ALG_21411_replaced([11156802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met,



then 5G-L2-PS shall schedule the PDSCH with subband beams.

else: 5G-L2-PS shall apply SRS based oDFT (5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB008322-E] /PMI [End CB008322-E]/SSB/refined beam (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if they are valid for UE’s PDSCH scheduling.

  * else: 5G-L2-PS shall apply SRS based oDFT (5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB008322-E] /PMI [End CB008322-E] /SSB/refined beam (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UE’s PDSCH scheduling and UE specific CSI- RS.  




[CB008322-E] For UEs under 8 ports mode, when beams used is not subband beams, port selection (5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for PDSCH rank 2 shall always be adopted. [End CB008322-E]

Note: For PDCCH transmission, the beam is the same as 5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when NRCELL/actDlSrsBm is true and UE is not subband beamforming enabled UE.

[End CB008322-A]

Note: beam ID of PDSCH, PDCCH for Paging/SI that has no UE specific info is not changed.

Note: PDCCH MAC CE indicating TCI status change is not updated based on beams from SRS because CSI-RS for tracking is still transmitted via SSB beam.

##### 3.2.6.4.1-1.0-3 Two beams for DL SUMIMO Four beams from SRS for 4-port UE specific CSI-RS resource (ID: 11112266)

**3.2.6.4.1-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11112276`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO [Before CB009527-A]

If the UE is subband beamforming enabled UE (5G_UP_ALG_21269_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

  * If all the criteria for subband BWVs usage defined in 5G_UP_ALG_21411_replaced([11156802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met,



If NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode is configured with "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "CL 8x4 MIMO":, then the wideband short-term CSI-RS beams shall be used for UE specific 4 port CSI-RS for channel acquisition.   


  * else: 5G-L2-PS shall apply SRS based oDFT (5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))/SSB/refined beam (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UE specific 4 port CSI-RS.



[CB009527-A]

For the subband beamforming enabled UE (5G_UP_ALG_21269_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with UE specific CSI-RS (4 ports):

\- If all criteria defined in 5G_UP_ALG_21411_replaced([11156802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met, 5G-L2-PS shall apply wideband short-term CSI-RS beams to CSI-RS for CSI.

\- Else, 5G-L2-PS shall apply SRS based oDFT (5G_UP_ALG_7278_replaced([11112223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))/SSB/refined beams (5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to CSI-RS for CSI.

[End CB009527-A]

##### 3.2.6.4.1-2.0-1 Two beams for DL SUMIMO [CB008577-A]TDD: [End CB008577-A] Extend two SSB/refinement beams to four beams for 8RX or 16RX receiver (ID: 11112283)

##### 3.2.6.4.1-2.0-2 Two beams for DL SUMIMO FDD: four beams for 8RX receiver (ID: 12771852)

**3.2.6.4.1-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12777197`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO If the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) : 

1) if NIDD:actPrachProbing is enabled: Four refined beams of the best beam from probing (refers to [11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ksgczpvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")) shall be indicated for PUSCH receiver [CB008577-C] before valid CSI report. After valid CSI report, best probing beam and its refinement information shall be set to invalid. 1x4 split of the latest best PMI beam shall be used. When CSI report is invalid and probing beam is invalid, fixed beamSet#4 shall be used. This policy shall be applied for both initial Tx and ReTx. [End CB008577-C]. 

2) if NIDD:actPrachProbing is disabled: Fixed beamSet#4 shall be indicated for PUSCH receiver [CB008577-C] before valid CSI report. After valid CSI report, 1x4 split of the latest best PMI beam shall be used. When CSI report is invalid, fixed beamSet#4 shall be used. This policy shall be applied for both initial Tx and ReTx. [End CB008577-C]. 

**Notes**

· FDD BF cells only supports NIDD NRCELL-numberOfRxBeamforming = 8 and numberOfRxPucch = 8

##### 3.2.6.4.1.0-1 Two beams for DL SUMIMO Two beams from beam report (ID: 11112198)

**3.2.6.4.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13458457`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO If for a given user two beams are reported, then:

  * L2-PS shall derive the 2nd target beam in the same way as the 1st target beam as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced([11112105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * L2-PS shall store the best beam as first beam.



If supercell is enabled a 2nd SSB beam reported is used for beam measurement metric calculation, also for dlMimoMode equal to "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO"**in TDD mode, L2-PS shall consider that PUCCH, PUSCH, PDCCH and PDSCH for a user are transmitted and received on a single virtual SSB beam.**

If for a given user two beams are applied for a transmission with dlMimoMode "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" (values 1,3) as defined in NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode:

  * L2-PS shall consider that PUCCH and PDCCH are also transmitted/received with dlMimoMode = 4x4.
  * L2-PS shall apply specific order of the two best beams (also after beam change) to PUSCH & PDSCH and to PDCCH, where the first XPolBeam is the best beam, as defined in 5G_L2_23011_replaced([11155919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248INvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * **NOTE1: 3GPP NR supports only beam indication of a single beam via TCI States with a single antenna panel which implies that the UE may measure frequency offset only of this single beam. Hence, if the two beams used for 4x4 MIMO come from opposite directions and the UE is moving fast this might lead then in worst case to call drops (in case of no Port selection for rank >2)**
  * **NOTE2: In dlMimoMode = 4x4 the actual control channel transmission mode is selected by L1. L2-PS shall set the parameters in such way that all modes can be supported.**



If numOfSubSectors == 2, only one beam is applied for a transmission with dlMimoMode = 4x4 as there is only one SSB beam per subsector. Only best beam is considered.

[Before CB013712-A]For PDCCH, if DL MU-MIMO is enabled (NRCELL/actDlMuMimo = True), only the best beam shall be used (PDCCH for an UE must be sent through its primary beam).[End CB013712-A]

When not in supercell mode, {the cell has dlMimoMode "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" } or {the cell has dlMimoMode "CL 8x4 MIMO"**and for the UEs under 4 ports mode}**], if the UE only reports one beam (nrOfReportedRS = n1 in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2684_replaced([11303281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqj_0PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), below behavior shall be as follow:****

When receives beam report, two beams are selected. If the best beam is same as the second best beam, the second best beam shall be changed to a random SSB beam which is not muted based on beamsMuted to ensure two beams are always different.

---

##### 3.2.6.4.1.0-2 Two beams for DL SUMIMO Two beams before valid beam report for 4x4 Mimo Mode (ID: 13464437)

**3.2.6.4.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11111593`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO **Two beams before valid beam report for 4x4 Mimo Mode**

After PRACH from an UE has been detected (5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and until there is report for the second best beam from this UE as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the second SSB beam used for 4x4 MIMO Mode is not used thanks to port selection. PatternId for this second beam is then set to the same as the first beam.

Until second best beam is available, parameter **pdschClPrecodingOption4X4 is set to value 2 independently of rdPdschClPrecodingOption4X4 (5G_L2_6956_replaced([11186551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276js_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value.**

pdschClPrecodingOption4X4 is **renamed pdschPrecodingOption4X4.**

If NRCELL/actDlMuMimo is true**, and if DL MIMO mode is 4xN (4 CSI-RS ports), L2-PS shall ensure the pdschPrecodingOption4x4 is set to value 2 independently of rdPdschPrecodingOption4x4 (5G_L2_6956_replaced([11186551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276js_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value.**

if NRCELL/numOfSubSectors == 2, only one SSB beam is applied in 4 _4 Mimo mode and port selection is not done (rdPdschPrecodingOption4X4 set to 0, see 5G_UP_ALG_3180_replaced([11139272](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3183_replaced([11139297](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Mapping in 4_4 Mimo mode in one sub sector between Beam ID and Pattern ID is described in 5G_UP_ALG_1924_replaced([11111609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOsAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 3.2.6.4.1.0-3 Two beams for DL SUMIMO TDD: Maximum Two beams from CSI feedback (ID: 11112211)

**3.2.6.4.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11112219`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO If dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false, for UEs with 8 port CSI-RS configured, beam pattern Id shall be computed from CSI feedback to select beam used for UE's PDSCH, PDCCH. Please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2201_replaced([11113014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * For PDSCH rank 2,3,4 transmission, the two PMI beams are arranged with the original reported order.

  * If NIDD:actDlMuMimo = True, for PDSCH at rank 2, port selection is always enabled. Only the best PMI beam (see 5G_UP_ALG_2201_replaced([11113014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used for PDSCH transmission at rank 2. About port selection at rank 2, please see 5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * For PDSCH rank 1, only 1 PMI beam is possible to be reported and shall be used.

  * For PDCCH of DL grant, the best PMI beam shall be used.




Before the first CSI feedback or CSI feedback is outdated, only 1 SSB beam is used, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3188_replaced([11139322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: beam ID of PDSCH, PDCCH for Paging/SI that has no UE specific info is not changed.

Note: PDCCH MAC CE indicating TCI status change is not updated based on CSI feedback because CSI-RS for tracking is still transmitted via SSB beam.

The beam for PDCCH is controlled by R&D parameter, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1984_replaced([11112043](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpSWYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true, which means [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] is greater than or equal to 4,

L2PS shall apply the beam pattern Id for UE's PDSCH only. For PDCCH, refer more to 5G_ALG_UP_9877.

If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" and [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] is greater than 4 in PCell or SCell, both UE specific and cell specific CSI-RS coexist for the cell,

L2 shall distinguish them and fill the beam index accordingly.

For the beam usage for UE specific CSI-RS resources, please refer 5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For the beam usage for cell specific CSI-RS resources, please refer 5G_UP_ALG_9731_replaced([11113316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 3.2.6.4.1.0-4 Two beams for DL SUMIMO FDD: Maximum Two beams from CSI feedback (ID: 12777257)

**3.2.6.4.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12777199`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO If the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) : 

Note PDCCH/PDSCH of Common channels SIB/Paging shall use DL full sector beam.

[Before CB008577-B] Before -B, dlMimoMode is "CL 4x4 MIMO" as WA before B ready. PMI beam is not available in this case. [End CB008577-B]

If dlMimoMode is "CL 32x4 MIMO", for UEs with 8/32 port CSI-RS configured, best and second best PMI beam pattern shall be computed from CSI feedback ([11112962: PMI beam change procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and be used for UE's DL and UL usage.

PDSCH

1) if NIDD:actPrachProbing is enabled: best beam from probing (refers to [11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ksgczpvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")) shall be indicated for PDSCH [CB008577-B] before valid CSI report. After valid CSI report, best probing beam information shall be set to invalid for DL [CB008577-C] and UL [End CB008577-C]. best PMI beam shall be used. When CSI report goes to invalid and probing beam is invalid, DL full sector beam shall be used. [End CB008577-B]. [Before CB008577-B] Before -B, if more than 1 beams needed, the duplication of same beam is filled. [End CB008577-B]

2) if NIDD:actPrachProbing is disabled: DL full sector beam shall be used for PDSCH [CB008577-B] before valid CSI report. After valid CSI report, PMI beam shall be used. When CSI report goes to invalid, full sector beam shall be used. [Before CB008577-B] Before -B, if more than 1 beams needed, the duplication of same beam is filled. [End CB008577-B]

When PMI beams is used:

  * For PDSCH rank 1, only 1 PMI beam is possible to be reported and shall be used.

  * For PDSCH rank 2: If port selection is enabled, only the best PMI beam shall be used for PDSCH transmission at rank 2. About port selection at rank 2, please see [11139421: Precoding matrix selection without adaptive rank](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krnRkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). If port selection is disabled, the two PMI beams are arranged with the original reported order.

  * For PDSCH rank 3,4 transmission, the two PMI beams are arranged with the original reported order.




PDCCH

if rdFddPdcchBeamType ([12806247: rdFddPdcchBeamType](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__jX58qAwEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is 0: full sector beam for DL shall be used;

else if rdFddPdcchBeamType is 1:

{

If best beam of #4 from probing is available, best beam of DL shall be used. 

else if PMI beams is valid: latest best PMI beam for DL shall be used. 

else, full sector beam for DL shall be used

}

else: NA;

Note: PDCCH grant for UL is handled in -C. This note does not need to be appear in the next rebase.

[End CB008577-B]

##### 3.2.6.4.1.0-5 Two beams for DL SUMIMO Two beams from SRS (ID: 11112223)

**3.2.6.4.1.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `12538353`)

Two beams for DL SUMIMO If UE is not subband beamforming enabled UE (5G_UP_ALG_21269_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If actDlSrsBm is true:

Two beams from periodic antenna switching usage SRS or codebook usage SRS shall be stored in Dl too, define them as SRS beams here. The beams are determined via 5G_UP_ALG_6995_replaced([11156011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (from antenna switch SRS resource set) or 5G_UP_ALG_2168_replaced([11154601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (from codebook SRS resource set). Whether the codebook usage SRS is used or not refers to 5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

If dlMimoMode "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" (values 1,3), beams for UE's PDCCH (both Ul grant and Dl grant) / PDSCH and UE specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition shall be:

If actDlSrsBm is true

For non-CA or UEs in Pcell, beams shall be determined by Dl BM state machine (5G_UP_ALG_6963_replaced([11155665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or Ul BM state machine (5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For UEs in Scell which have valid DFT beams iinformation from Pcell, beams shall be determinded by beams information from Pcell. 

[Before CNI-137616-A] If rdDisableBestSrsBeamForPdcch [5G_UP_ALG_14772_replaced([11114093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kphm4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] = true, then [End CNI-137616-A] the best SSB beam reported by UE shall be used for PDCCH. [Before CNI-137616-A] Otherwise the beam determined above shall be used for PDCCH. [End CNI-137616-A]

else

Legacy works as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2025_replaced([11112198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

If dlMimoMode "CL 8x4 MIMO", beams for UE's PDCCH/PDSCH and UE specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition shall be:

If actDlSrsBm is true

For non-CA or UEs in Pcell, beams shall be determined by Dl BM state machine (5G_UP_ALG_6963_replaced([11155665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or Ul BM state machine (5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For UEs in Scell which have valid DFT beams iinformation from Pcell, beams shall be determinded by beams information from Pcell. 

For UEs with 8 port cell specific CSI-RS, port selection (5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for PDSCH rank 2 shall always be adopted.

[Before CNI-137616-A] If rdDisableBestSrsBeamForPdcch = true, then [End CNI-137616-A] the best SSB beam reported by UE shall be used for PDCCH. [Before CNI-137616-A] Otherwise the beam determined above shall be used for PDCCH. [End CNI-137616-A]

else

Legacy works as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2028_replaced([11112211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Beams for cell specific CSI-RS for channel acquisition shall not be changed.

If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = true:

\- For UEs which are configured with 4-port CSI-RS, rank 4 port selection shall be enabled (see 5G_UP_ALG_3180_replaced([11139272](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

\- For UEs which are configured with 8-port CSI-RS, rank 2 port selection shall be enabled (see 5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Note, to trigger rank 2 port selection, the numStreamIndex in streamConfig shall be set to 2, about definition of streamConfig, see 5G_L1_IF_15591_replaced([11512962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteY_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details.

\- With port selection, PDSCH shall only be transmitted with one x-pol beam (the best beam) when UE's rank is not higher than 2.

\- Some background information about why port selection shall be enabled for DL MU-MIMO can be found via the link: [https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008305%20DL%20MU-MIMO%20Enhancement/Reference%20Documents/Layer%20based%20MU-SINR%20estimation.pptx?d=w3bca1c68e9b04123bdf241724c0e3e20&csf=1&web=1&e=y3DImo](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008305%20DL%20MU-MIMO%20Enhancement/Reference%20Documents/Layer%20based%20MU-SINR%20estimation.pptx?d=w3bca1c68e9b04123bdf241724c0e3e20&csf=1&web=1&e=y3DImo)

Else if UE is subband beamforming enabled UE (5G_UP_ALG_21269_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

DL beams shall be applied to PDSCH and UE specific CSI-RS as in 5G_UP_ALG_13891_replaced([11112241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). (note: TCI MAC CE for beam change shall not be triggered). For other transmissions such as PDCCH, other CSI-RS (CSI), PUCCH,

PUSCH, and to AP-SRS, subband beams shall not be used but beams shall be used as defined above in this

requirement.

Note: beam ID of PDSCH, PDCCH for Paging/SI that has no UE specific info is not changed.

Note: PDCCH MAC CE indicating TCI status change is not updated based on CSI feedback because CSI-RS for tracking is still transmitted via SSB beam.

#### 3.2.6.5.0-2 Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels Apply Updated Beam ID to 4RX Physical Channels (ID: 11112337)

**3.2.6.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11112342`)

Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels If eCPRI FD BF is enabled and UL subcell configured with 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

{

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_25049_replaced([11112337](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUyoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Two UL beams shall be used for PUSCH, short PUCCH & A-SRS. The serving beam is used as first UL beam, the second UL beam shall be as same as second DL best beam according to UE report. Before the first beam update is triggered, the beam Id associated to the RACH resources shall be used as first UL beam in which the last UE's RACH preamble was received as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Before first beam update is triggered or if second DL best beam is not available, the second UL beam shall be a random neighbor beam of the first UL beam. If appliedUlBeamSweeping = TRUE or appliedUlBeamFallback = TRUE, the UL beam selection is determined by 5G_UP_ALG_2040_replaced([11112412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_2061_replaced([11112525](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). IF PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==True), SSB beams shall be used, and 2nd SSB beam shall be different than the 1st one. See 5G_UP_ALG_2218_replaced([11113106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5MvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details. PUSCH data can be still received over refined beams, if applicable.

Note: The detailed algorithm to select random neighbor beam is determined by CP3.

[Before PR733202]

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 4 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UE is configured with 2 SSB beams and beam refinement is disabled for the UE and periodic SRS is not configured for the UE , the two SSB beams shall be directly used on all UL channels except PRACH(which uses duplicated beams).

[PR733202]

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 4 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams:

\- For PUSCH, if beam refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE , the two SSB beams shall be used on PUSCH.

\- For PUCCH F3&F1, the two SSB beams shall be used on it no matter beam refinement is enabled or disabled or SRS beams are valid or not.

\- For PRACH, duplicated beams shall be used.

[End PR733202]

}

#### 3.2.6.5.0-3 Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels Apply Updated Beam ID to 8RX Physical Channels (ID: 11112346)

**3.2.6.5.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12771859`)

Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels [CB008577-A] If NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'TDD': {

[End CB008577-A] If eCPRI FD BF is enabled and PUSCH, long PUCCH, A-SRS & periodic SRS for measurement is received over 8 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

{

Four UL beams shall be used for PUSCH, long PUCCH, A-SRS & periodic SRS for measurement.

1\. For PUSCH, A-SRS & periodic SRS for measurement, before SRS beams selected in 5G_UP_ALG_20242_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are available,

\- IF the number of beams in UE context is one, L2PS shall find 4 beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- ELSE L2PS shall select two best beams stored in UE context and one correlated beam for each best beam according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  1. For PUCCH, if PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==True) AND NRBTS/NRCELL.numberOfRxPucch is equal to 8, only SSB coarse beams shall be used to receive PUCCH. The detailed algorithm please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2214_replaced([11113079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



**NOTE:**

1) If NRBTS/NRCELL.numberOfRxPucch is equal to 4, the SSB coarse beams used to receive PUCCH shall the same as the ones in eCPRI C4 UL subcell with FD BF enabled.

2) Only long pucch is supported and short pucch is out of scope.

3) Beam sweeping shall be disabled (appliedUlBeamSweeping = false) according to 5G_UP_ALG_2097_replaced([11112645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX17PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

4) In case that the number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 8(5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) _, if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams (NIDD:NRBTS.NRCELLGRP.numberOfBeams = 2):_

\- For PUSCH, if refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE , the two SSB beams in the configured beamSet shall be extending by 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the 4 beams shall be used.

\- For PUCCH F3, the extension SSB beams (2 SSB beams in the configured beamSet -->4 SSB beams) shall be used on PUCCH if it is received over 8 streams no matter beam refinement is enabled or not OR SRS beams are valid or not. For PUCCH F1, sector beam shall be used according to 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Quater sector beams shall be used if it is received over 8 streams.

\- For PRACH, the duplicated beams shall be used.

Note: 1) If PUCCH F1 & F3 is received over 4 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two SSB beams reported from UE side shall be used as legacy.

}

Else if rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60:

{

Four UL panel split beams (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_32388_replaced([11113948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used for PUSCH, long PUCCH, A-SRS for SU MIMO.

}

[CB008577-A] }

If NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'FDD': {

If the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PUSCH (including A-SRS), long PUCCH is received over 8 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): 

  * For PRACH, 



1) if NIDD:actPrachProbing is enabled: gNB-DU shall indicate 4 beams within the internal beamSet#4 for UL. 

2) if NIDD:actPrachProbing is disabled: the fullSectorBeampatternId for UL shall be indicated for the duplicated streams.

  * For PUCCH F1 and F3, refers to [12770624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JBaoA4iTEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9);

  * For PUSCH refers to [12771852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__UhkgYlZEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).




}

[End CB008577-A]

#### 3.2.6.5.0-4 Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels Apply Updated Beam ID to 16RX Physical Channels (ID: 11112363)

**3.2.6.5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11112367`)

Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels If eCPRI FD BF is enabled and PUSCH, long PUCCH, A-SRS & periodic SRS for measurement is received over 16 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

{

1\. For PUSCH, A-SRS & periodic SRS for measurement, before SRS beams selected in 5G_UP_ALG_20242_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are available,

\- L2PS shall select 8 beams or 4 beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_27355_replaced([11113592](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  1. For PUCCH, if PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==True) AND NRBTS/NRCELL.numberOfRxPucch is equal to 8, only SSB coarse beams shall be used to receive PUCCH. The detailed algorithm please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2214_replaced([11113079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



**NOTE:**

1) If NRBTS/NRCELL.numberOfRxPucch is equal to 4, the SSB coarse beams used to receive PUCCH shall the same as the ones in eCPRI C4 UL subcell with FD BF enabled.

2) Only long pucch is supported and short pucch is out of scope.

3) Beam sweeping shall be disabled (appliedUlBeamSweeping = false) according to 5G_UP_ALG_2097_replaced([11112645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX17PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

}

---

#### 3.2.6.5.0-5 Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels Usage of Sector Beam for PUCCH (ID: 11112372)

**3.2.6.5.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11112388`)

Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels For the case that FD beamforming is not enabled, if NRCELL/actDlMuMimo is true, the UL beam for receiving HARQ feedback over short PUCCH shall be switched to the sector beam. The pattern ID of sector beam is provided by the parameter halfSectorBeamPatternId/ fullSectorBeamPatternId in bfSetup (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2480_replaced([11288965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2483_replaced([11289095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-xBfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If FD beamforming is not enabled then

If more than one UEs’ CSI feedback in one symbol need to be received in one UL subcell and these users have different beams, the UL beam for that subcell shall be switched to the sector beam. The pattern ID of sector beam is provided by the parameter halfSectorBeamPatternId/ fullSectorBeamPatternId in bfSetup (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2480_replaced([11288965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2483_replaced([11289095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-xBfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 

Note : FD BF not enabled implies that either (dlEcpriFdBeamforming && ulEcpriFdBeamforming) is false or actFdmEnhancedScheduling is false

If FD beamforming is enabled (ulEcpriFdBeamforming==True, 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2525_replaced([11297471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqGs3_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND Long PUCCH is used for FR1 TDD AND PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the usage of sector beam for Long PUCCH is defined by 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note. In particular cases, different meanings of "sector beam" can be considered:

  * 4 quarter-sector beams can be combined into single 8RX sector beam used for PUCCH Format 1 resources if PUCCH is received over 8 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * two half-sector beams can be combined into single 4RX sector beam used for PUCCH Format 1 resources if PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * single full-sector beam can be used as 2nd Xpol of 4RX receiver for PUCCH Format 3 resources if PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).




The sector beam patternID is obtained as follows:

If NRBTS/NRCELL/numOfSubSectors >0, the sector beam patternID is provided in 5G_UP_ALG_1924_replaced([11111609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOsAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Else, the patternId of sector beam is provided by the parameters fullSectorBeamPatternId/halfSectorBeamPatternId in bfSetup (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2480_replaced([11288965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 2483 and 5G_UP_ALG_2218_replaced([11113106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5MvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). NOTE: New IE may be needed and it will be decided in CP3 for 8RX.End

In case of UCA cell (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1-TDD, eCPRI, UL sub-cells with four spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , same UL beam selection is performed for all UL channels according to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and PUCCH in C4 case shall be configured with the same UL specific beams as other UL channels, instead of sector beam (see 5G_UP_ALG_6_replaced([11094165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmaBcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2475_replaced([11288953](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp9i9vvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 4 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams:

\- For PUSCH, if beam refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE , the two SSB beams shall be used on PUSCH.

\- For PUCCH F3&F1, the two SSB beams shall be used on it no matter beam refinement is enabled or disabled or SRS beams are valid or not.

\- For PRACH, duplicated beams shall be used.

In case that the number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 8 or 16 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams(NIDD:NRBTS.NRCELLGRP.numberOfBeams = 2):

\- For PUSCH, if refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE , the two SSB beams in the configured beamSet shall be extending by 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the 4 beams shall be used.

\- For PUCCH F3, the extension SSB beams (2 SSB beams in the configured beamSet -->4 SSB beams) shall be used on PUCCH if it is received over 8 streams no matter beam refinement is enabled or not OR SRS beams are valid or not. For PUCCH F1, sector beam shall be used according to 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Quater sector beams shall be used if it is received over 8 streams.

\- For PRACH, the duplicated beams shall be used.

Note: 1) If PUCCH F1 & F3 is received over 4 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two SSB beams reported from UE side shall be used as legacy.

[CB013442-D]

If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_32388_replaced([11113948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detail four beams for PUCCH F1 & F3.

[End CB013442-D]

#### 3.2.6.5.0-6 Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels Apply Updated beam based on Beam report (ID: 12793840)

**3.2.6.5.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12793842`)

Apply Updated Beam ID to Physical Channels [CB008577-A] Note: just split legacy req to smaller ones, no change to beam report [End CB008577-A] 

An updated beam ID shall be applied to PDCCH, PDSCH, CSI-RS (CSI), PUCCH, PUSCH, and to AP-SRS for SU-MIMO when MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication is HARQ ACKed or finally HARQ NACKed plus a fixed delay if The MAC CE is triggered, the timing refer to 5G_UP_ALG_29442_replaced([11112392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If for a given user two beams are applied for a transmission and first beam has changed then new 2nd beam shall be taken into use with the same timing as 1st beam.

If for a given user two beams are applied for a transmission and only 2nd beam has changed then then new 2nd beam shall be updated immediately.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
scenario |  | 1st beam |  | 2nd beam |  | Time when new beam is used |  |   
1. |  | remains |  | changes |  | Just after the report or measured. |  |   
| 2. |  | changes |  | remains |  | After MAC-CE HARQ feedback |   
| 3. |  | changes |  | changes |  | After MAC-CE HARQ feedback |   
| 4. |  | Remains |  | remains |  | NA |   
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |   
  
**Figure. Overview of beam change scenarios**

**Note: Beam change indication is needed also in FR1 e.g. in order to enable the UE to measure the TRS resources corresponding to the serving beam.**

**Note: Alternative optimization: event triggered delay for PDSCH after CSI feedback on target beam is received and for PUSCH after SRS is measured on target beam. If event is not triggered after a timeout, target beam shall be applied.**

**NOTE: the beam selection is impacted if _appliedUlBeamSweeping = TRUE (5G_L2_1240_replaced([11183670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMi_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if _appliedUlBeamFallback = TRUE (5G_L2_1238_replaced([11183760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lzn_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), or if _appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange= TRUE (5G_L2_1244_replaced([11183675](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMjPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))._****

Before the first beam update is triggered, the beam Id associated to the RACH resources shall be used in which the last UE's RACH preamble was received as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Beam update shall be triggered based on Beam report on UCI.

If an updated refined beam has the same related SSB index as the serving beam, the updated beam ID shall be immediately applied just after the report to PDCCH, PDSCH, CSI-RS (CSI), PUCCH, PUSCH, and to AP-SRS for SU-MIMO. This shall be valid for the 1st beam and the 2nd beam if for a given user two beams are applied.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
scenario |  | 1st beam |  | 2nd beam |  | Time when new beam is used (with same related SSB as the serving beam) |  |   
1. |  | remains |  | Changes |  | Just after the report or measured. |  |   
| 1a. |  | changes |  | Remains |  | Just after the report or measured. |   
| 1b. |  | changes |  | Changes |  | Just after the report or measured. |   
| 4. |  | Remains |  | Remains |  | NA |   
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |   
  
**Table. Overview of fine beam change scenarios if related SSB remains.**
