### 3.2.6.6 Beam fallback for UL

#### 3.2.6.6.0-1 Beam fallback for UL UL Beam probing and fallback (ID: 11112416)

**3.2.6.6.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11112438`)

Beam fallback for UL In _appliedUlBeamFallback == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):_

If a target beam was not defined by a beam report, the procedures of uplink beam fallback as defined by this requirement (5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be conducted.

Note:

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO:beam for UL receiver shall still be from Beam report, the procedures of uplink beam fallback as defined by this requirement and retrigger UL fall back procedure defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2051_replaced([11112493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall still be conducted based on SSB/refined beam changing from beam report.

For UEs which are configured with periodic SRS and state machine for BM is NOT under the state of SRS_BM_AGED (see 5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UL beam fallback and probing algorithms shall be skipped because UL beams are selected based on periodic SRS but not beam reports from UEs.

For FR1 SCell with UL configured according to 5G_UP_ALG_2698_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), UL beam fallback and probing algorithms shall be conducted.

**[CB014005-A] When SSB/refined beam set is online updated, the target beam is selected by the first beam report after beam set update (5G_UP_ALG_32949_replaced([11112143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the procedures of uplink beam probing and fallback as defined by the requirements (5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_10371_replaced([11112443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be conducted. **[End CB014005-A]****

If number of spatial streams for a given UL subcell is 2 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**Probing**

The old UL source beam ID shall be stored in UE context before the UL beam changes. Instantaneous SINR values of a) the last scheduled UL slot before and b) the first scheduled UL slot after an updated beam ID is applied shall be measured and stored in the UE context.

**NOTE: an updated beam ID shall be applied when a MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication is HARQ ACKed or finally HARQ NACKed plus a fixed delay = 3ms.**

**NOTE: updated beam PMI ID application shall not be impacted by MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication is HARQ ACKed or finally HARQ NACKed.**

If the UL SINR value of the new beam ID is better than the value of the old beam ID or the PUSCH on old beam is DTX'ed, then the new beam ID shall be applied further as serving UL beam for PUCCH Format 3, PUSCH, and to AP-SRS for SU-MIMO.

Normalized SINR values, as in 5G_UP_ALG_2048_replaced([11112469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), shall be compared.

**UL Beam Fallback**

If SINR of the new candidate beam is equal or lower than the SINR value of the old beam, **or the PUSCH on new candidate beam is DTX'ed, the old beam ID shall be applied in next slots for PUCCH, PUSCH, and to AP-SRS for SU-MIMO. If the UL beam falls back to the old beam ID, this shall be conducted directly in the next slot without any latency and without signaling to the UE.**

else 

5G-L2-PS shall conduct UL Beam probing and fallback ~~for C4 ulSubcellType~~ as in 5G_UP_ALG_10371_replaced([11112443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).~~5G-L2-PS shall conduct UL Beam probing and fallback as in 5G_UP_ALG_10371_replaced([11112443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).~~

Endif

5G-L2-PS shall apply beam pattern Ids to physical channels including Long PUCCH as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2031_replaced([11112294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUyl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and in 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**NOTE: In case of UCA cell (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1-TDD, eCPRI, ~~C4~~ UL sub-cells with 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), _appliedUlBeamFallback shall be *FALSE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and UL beam selection is performed according to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and does not rely on beam report._***

**NOTE: Any UL symbols between above two UL slots, e.g., PUCCH symbols in special slots, shall use the serving beam as defined without the PR4830646. That is old beam ID shall be applied if before the updated beam ID is applied. The new beam ID shall be applied after that point in time.**

**NOTE: UL slots used for (re-)probing are not considered by to OLLA and ILLA, see 5G_UP_ALG_3078_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 5G_UP_ALG_3153_replaced([11137866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krcScfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**NOTE: PM counters NR Beamforming/UL_SERV_BEAM_ID_BEAM_xx (M55305C010xx) shall be updated with current serving beam for all probing allocations (i.e. not with the beam which is probed)**.****

If UE is configured for skippable grants (5G_UP_ALG_4839_replaced([11195286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7J1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), any PUSCH DTX indication shall be managed per 5G_UP_ALG_16415_replaced([11195380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7w7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.2.6.6.0-2 Beam fallback for UL UL Beam probing and fallback (ID: 11112443)

**3.2.6.6.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11112456`)

Beam fallback for UL This requirement shall apply to UL subcell configured with 4 or 8 [CB010708-C] or 16 [End CB010708-C] spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Two old source beam IDs shall be stored in UE context before the beam changes. Before the new candidate beam is used, it shall be probed with a PUSCH request to check the SINR of the new beam. Only one new candidate beam (different than the beams stored in UE context) is probed every time, by keeping the old best beam and replace second best beam as new candidate beam. If there are two new candidate beams derived from UE report, the probing may need to be performed twice to determine the finally two best UL beams. If there’s no new candidate beam IDs derived from UE report, probing is not performed while the old beams remained.

If UL subcell configured with 8 [CB010708-C] or 16 [End CB010708-C] spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the number of SSB/refinement beams reported from UE side is still two. L2PS shall extend the number of SSB/refinement beams in UE context from two to four according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and send it to gNB-L1. The SINR for the new beam which is used in probing shall be the averaged SINR over the corresponding two extended beams (5G_UP_ALG_2049_replaced([11112474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Initially only one beam is stored in UE context, it is SSB beam corresponding to received PRACH message, later two different beam IDs are updated based on UE report. If beam refinement is enabled, once UE reports a different candidate beam and at least one SSB beam is recorded in UE context, all SSB beam(s) recorded in UE context shall be erased before the probing (i.e. If there’s one refined beam recorded in UE context, it shall be used as the only old UL beam for probing, otherwise the new reported beam(s) shall be directly used without probing). Before UE reports a different candidate beam, or if UE reports only one candidate beam and there’s no beam Id recorded in UE context after SSB beam erasure, the randomly selected or the extended UL beam is used for UL channel reception but the random or extended beam is not recorded on UE context for beam probing purpose. Note: The detailed algorithm to select random second UL beam is determined by CP3.

Normalized beam specific SINR values of a) the last scheduled UL slot before and b) the first scheduled UL slot and later slots after an updated beam ID is applied shall be measured and stored in the UE context. Definition of Beam specific SINR is described in 5G_UP_ALG_2049_replaced([11112474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: an updated beam ID shall be applied when a MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication is HARQ ACKed or finally HARQ NACKed plus a fixed delay = 3ms.

NOTE: updated beam PMI ID application shall not be impacted by MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication is HARQ ACKed or finally HARQ NACKed.

For every probing, two different beams among old and new candidate beams with highest SINR values shall be selected as first and second UL beams, the corresponding beam IDs and SINR values shall be recorded in UE context once the new beams are selected. If UL subcell is configured with 8 [CB010708-C] or 16 [End CB010708-C]spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2PS shall extend two SSB/refinement beams to four beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). These beams shall be used directly in PUCCH Format 3 and if actLongPucchF1F3BfOnOranExtT6 is True, then PUCCH F1 and PUCCH F3,PUSCH, and AP-SRS;

In any probing if PUSCH measurement is DTX, the new candidate beam used in probed PUSCH shall not be selected and recorded in UE context irrespective of its SINR value.

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 4 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams:

  * For PUSCH, if beam refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE , the two SSB beams shall be used on PUSCH.

  * For PUCCH F3&F1, the two SSB beams shall be used on it no matter beam refinement is enabled or disabled or SRS beams are valid or not.

  * For PRACH, duplicated beams shall be used.




In case that the number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 8 [CB010708-C] or 16 [End CB010708-C](5G_UP_8362_replaced\(\[11388556\]\(https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ\)\)) , if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams(NIDD:NRBTS.NRCELLGRP.numberOfBeams = 2):

  * For PUSCH, if refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE , the two SSB beams in the configured beamSet shall be extending by 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the 4 beams shall be used.

  * For PUCCH F3, the extension SSB beams (2 SSB beams in the configured beamSet -->4 SSB beams) shall be used on PUCCH if it is received over 8 streams no matter beam refinement is enabled or not OR




SRS beams are valid or not. For PUCCH F1, sector beam shall be used according to 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Quater sector beams shall be used if it is received over 8 streams.

  * For PRACH, the duplicated beams shall be used.



Note: 1) If PUCCH F1 & F3 is received over 4 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two SSB beams reported from UE side shall be used as legacy.

---

#### 3.2.6.6.0-5 Beam fallback for UL Beam specific SINR measurement (ID: 11112474)

**3.2.6.6.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11112487`)

Beam fallback for UL If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams for a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the instantaneous beam specific SINR value shall be based on the SINR (in dB) of the measured rx antenna stream ((refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1704_replaced([11108993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koyACfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

sinrOfAnt: the Sinr value of measured rx antenna stream.

instSinrSlot[i, j]_dB = 10*log10((10^(sinrOfAnt[ant1]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant2]/10)) / 2), where i is the index of the slots, j is the beam ID, ant1 and ant2 are the antenna index corresponding to beam j.

If PUSCH is received over 8 [Before CB010708-D] or 16 [ CB010708-D] spatial streams for a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G_UP_ALG_27595_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to 8, OR rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G_UP_ALG_27595_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to 16 but the number of SSB beams stored in UE context is one (note: 8RX receiver will be used in this case), [End CB010708-D] , the instantaneous beam specific SINR value shall be based on the SINR (in dB) of the measured rx antenna stream (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1704_replaced([11108993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koyACfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

instSinrSlot[i, j]_dB = 10*log10((10^(sinrOfAnt[ant1]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant2]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant3]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant4]/10)) / 4), where, ant1 and ant2 are the antenna index corresponding to the extended beam x, ant3 and ant4 are the antenna index corresponding to extended beam y. For each SSB/refinement beam, two corelated beams shall be found according to one(SSB beam j)-to-two(corelated beams x and y) mapping relationship in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_11171_replaced([11297028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqGFwfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB010708-D]

If PUSCH is received over 16 spatial streams for a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G_UP_ALG_27595_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to 16 AND the number of SSB beams stored in UE context is two , the instantaneous beam specific SINR value shall be based on the SINR (in dB) of the measured rx antenna stream (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1704_replaced([11108993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koyACfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

instSinrSlot[i, j]_dB = 10*log10((10^(sinrOfAnt[ant1]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant2]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant3]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant4]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant5]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant6]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant7]/10) + 10^(sinrOfAnt[ant8]/10)) / 8),

[End CB010708-D]

If two instantaneous beam specific SINR values are compared, normalized beam specific SINR values shall be used when comparing the old and the new candidate beam.

If 5G-L2-PS measures SINR on PUSCH, the SINR value is normalized to the number of PRBs such that:

normSinrSlot[i, j]_dB = instSinrSlot[i, j]_dB + 10 * log10(numPuschPrb_i)

where numPuschPrb_i is the number of PRBs in the ith UL slot and beam j.

Note: instSinrSlot and normSinrSlot shall be maintained per UE.

Note: 5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL Beam probing and fallback) calls for ignoring PUSCH DTX for grants types listed in that requirement when UE is configured for skippable grants (5G_UP_ALG_4839_replaced([11195286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7J1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for 5GC0002271-B) . Do to L2 PS implementation of this requirement, it would be easier to also skip the normalized beam specific SINR calculation. Therefore the normalized beam specific SINR calculation referred to above can be skipped in this case.

---

#### 3.2.6.6.0-6 Beam fallback for UL Re-Probing (ID: 11112493)

**3.2.6.6.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11112500`)

Beam fallback for UL In appliedUlBeamFallback == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If a UL beam falls back to old beam IDs, regularly the serving DL beams shall be probed as UL beams if a UE is scheduled on PUSCH but only if SINR value of the old beam IDs are measured after the latest beam fall back.

If NRBTS-actBeamControlImprovement2 == False: 5G-L2-PS shall set rdUlBeamProbingCounterInSlots = 15. 

NOTE: The 2nd serving UL beam can be triggered to be updated by a DL beam report.

Condition A: For a given UE, the UL beams falls back to the old beam IDs (5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), that are the serving UL beam IDs which are not include the best serving DL beam ID.

Condition B: a given UE is scheduled in PUSCH at least after K UL slots latest beam fall back. Where K is the number of UL slots defined by the parameter rdUlBeamProbingCounter_slots as defined in 5G_L2_1239_replaced([11183765](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lzoPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Condition C: old beam IDs were used and their beam SINR values were measured and stored after the latest beam fall back.

If all conditions A, B, & C are full filled, the serving DL beam IDs shall be used as UL beam IDs and the SINR values shall be measured, as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 Mimo and PMI beam is used for DL, only SSB/refined beam in DL UE context will be updated, PMI beam for DL is not changed by this.

Note: If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams for a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two beam IDs are used with beam specific SINR(5G_UP_ALG_2049_replaced([11112474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); otherwise only one beam ID is used with UE specific SINR(5G_UP_ALG_2047_replaced([11112462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: For UEs which are configured with periodic SRS and state machine for BM is NOT under the state of SRS_BM_AGED (see 5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UL beam re-probing algorithm shall be skipped because UL beams are selected based on periodic SRS but not on beam reports from UEs.

[Before PR733202]

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 4 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UE is configured with 2 SSB beams and beam refinement is disabled for the UE and periodic SRS is not configured for the UE , the two SSB beams shall be directly used on all UL channels except PRACH(which uses duplicated beams).

[PR733202]

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 4 (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams:

\- For PUSCH, if beam refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for the UE, the two SSB beams shall be used on PUSCH.

\- For PUCCH F3&F1, the two SSB beams shall be used on it no matter beam refinement is enabled or disabled or SRS beams are valid or not.

\- For PRACH, duplicated beams shall be used.

[End PR733202]

[CB009363-I]

[Before PR733202]

If number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 8(5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UE is configured with 2 SSB beams and beam refinement is disabled for the UE and periodic SRS is not configured for the UE, the four SSB beams after extension according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be directly used on all UL channels except PRACH(which uses duplicated beams).

[PR733202]

In case that the number of spatial streams for a given ul subcell is 8(5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , if UE is configured with 2 SSB beams(NIDD:NRBTS.NRCELLGRP.numberOfBeams = 2):

\- For PUSCH, if refinement is disabled and no valid SRS beams for this UE , the two SSB beams in the configured beamSet shall be extending by 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the 4 beams shall be used.

\- For PUCCH F3, the extension SSB beams (2 SSB beams in the configured beamSet -->4 SSB beams) (5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used on PUCCH if it is received over 8 streams no matter beam refinement is enabled or not OR SRS beams are valid or not. For PUCCH F1, sector beam shall be used according to 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Quater sector beams shall be used if it is received over 8 streams.

\- For PRACH, the duplicated beams shall be used.

Note: 1) If PUCCH F1 & F3 is received over 4 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two SSB beams reported from UE side shall be used as legacy.

[End PR733202]

[End CB009363-I]

NOTE: Depending on the ratio of UL slots scheduled and not scheduled to a given UE, from every 10th UL slot (peak rate: all UL slots scheduled to a given UE) to every 2nd UL slot (every Nth UL slot is scheduled to a given UE, with N >= 10) is used for re-probing the UL beam.

Function as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be conducted for measuring UL SINR on different beams even if DL beam ID does not change.

If DL beam changes, 1st probing as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) overwrites re-probing triggered as defined in this requirement.

NOTE: The value rdUlBeamProbingCounter_slots should be roughly followed. FT can decide if this is implemented by a timer which duration is calculated by rdUlBeamProbingCounter_slots divided by the UL slot rate as defined by the frame structure.

NOTE: UL slots used for (re-)probing are not considered by to OLLA and ILLA, see 5G_UP_ALG_3078_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 5G_UP_ALG_3153_replaced([11137866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krcScfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: PM counters NR Beamforming/UL_SERV_BEAM_ID_BEAM_xx (M55305C010xx) shall be updated with current serving beam for all probing allocations (i.e. not with the beam which is probed).

### 3.2.6.7 Beam fallback for DL

#### 3.2.6.7.0-1 Beam fallback for DL UL Beam Probing Before DL Beam Change (ID: 11112507)

**3.2.6.7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11112523`)

Beam fallback for DL In _appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):_

If a target beam was not defined by a beam report, the procedures of uplink beam probing before downlink beam change as defined by this requirement (5G_UP_ALG_2056_replaced([11112507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be conducted.

For FR1 CA **UE with TDD Scell beamforming activated and SCell DL configured only according to 5G_UP_ALG_2698_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the procedure of uplink beam probing before downlink beam changes shall not be conducted over TDD Scell.**

**[CB014005-A] When SSB/refined beam set is online updated, the target beam is selected by the first beam report after beam set update (5G_UP_ALG_32949_replaced([11112143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the procedures of uplink beam fallback as defined by the requirements (5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_10371_replaced([11112443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be conducted. **[End CB014005-A]****

If the number of spatial streams to receive PUSCH(5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 2 in a given UL subcell:

If in 5G_UP_ALG_2047_replaced([11112462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) normSinrSlot[i+k]_db < normSinrSlot[i]_db and if the normSinrSlot[i]_db - normSinrSlot[i+k]_db > _rdSinrDiffNewAndOldBeam (5G_L2_1246_replaced([11183681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMjfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), where slot[i] is the latest one in which the old beam is used and slot[i+k] the one in which the candidate beam is used, 5G-L2-PS shall NOT conduct DL beam change and shall keep DL serving beam in the UE context which should be applied for PDCCH, PDSCH, and CSI-RS (CSI)__. Otherwise 5G-L2-PS shall conduct DL beam change._ **

If the number of spatial streams to receive PUSCH(5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is **NOT equal to 2 in a given UL subcell:**

If in 5G_UP_ALG_2049_replaced([11112474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) normSinrSlot[i+k, j2]_db < normSinrSlot[i, j1]_db and if the normSinrSlot[i, j1]_db - normSinrSlot[i+k, j2]_db > _rdSinrDiffNewAndOldBeam (5G_L2_1246_replaced([11183681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMjfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), where slot[i] is the latest one in which the old beams are used and slot[i+k] the one in which the best candidate beam is used, j1 is the best old beam, j2 is the best candidate beam, 5G-L2-PS shall NOT conduct DL beam change and shall keep DL serving beam in the UE context which should be applied for PDCCH, PDSCH, and CSI-RS (CSI)__. Otherwise 5G-L2-PS shall conduct DL beam change._ **

**NOTE: In case of UCA cell (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1-TDD, eCPRI, ~~C4~~ UL subcell with 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), _appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange shall be *FALSE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and UL beam selection is performed according to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and does not rely on beam report._***

If a second best beam is used in DL, 5G-L2-PS shall also fallback the second best beam to old second best beam. 5G-L2-PS must not apply the same beam Id as first beam and second beam.

NOTE: PM counters NR Beamforming/DL_SERV_BEAM_ID_BEAM_xx (M55305C000xx) shall be updated with current serving beam for all probing allocations (i.e. not with the beam which is probed)

Note: If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO: _appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange related function is the same as before,_ L2 still checked UL sinr based on DL beam report, still change DL serving beam in the UE context based on beam probing result. Because CSI-RS for tracking is still transmitted via SSB beams and PUCCH/PUSCH is still received via SSB/refined beams. Especially PDCCH/PDSCH will also use SSB/refined beams when CSI feedback is out of date.**

**NOTE: appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange should not be TRUE if appliedUlBeamFallback set to FALSE.**

---

### 3.2.6.8 UL beam sweeping

#### 3.2.6.8.1 UL beam sweeping

#### 3.2.6.8.1-1 UL beam sweeping

##### 3.2.6.8.1-1.0-1 UL beam sweeping Condition: if SINR(candidate beam) &gt; SINR(used UL beam) + rdSweepingSinrOffset_dB (5G_L2_1243_replaced( 11183703 )). Where "used UL beam" means  the best UL beam recorded in UE database when beam sweeping is triggered, or the new selected DL serving beam if this criteria is met with another candidate beam previously. If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell(5G_UP_8362_replaced( 11388556 )), the SINR comparision shall be based on beam specific SINR (see 5G_UP_ALG_2049_replaced( 11112474 )) values, and the compared beams shall be the second UL beam (equals to the candidate beam) and the first UL beam ( equal to the used UL beam) which are used on the same swept slot. (ID: 11112667)

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-1 UL beam sweeping Overview (ID: 11112532)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11112535`)

UL beam sweeping The gNB shall support UL beam sweeping in following functions:

  * Order of beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2071_replaced([11112539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWn2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Rate of beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2073_replaced([11112549](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWn3_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Channels measured for beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2075_replaced([11112558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpXO0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Method of measurement for beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2078_replaced([11112568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpXO3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Application of the beam sweeping measurements outcome to UL channels and signals (5G_UP_ALG_2080_replaced([11112575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpXO4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Application of the beam sweeping measurements outcome to DL channels and signals (5G_UP_ALG_2082_replaced([11112583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpXO4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Stopping beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2084_replaced([11112591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpXO5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Skipping UL fallback function upon triggering of beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2086_replaced([11112599](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpXO6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Resuming UL fallback function upon finishing the beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2088_replaced([11112606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX14fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Difference between the best and the second best beam (5G_UP_ALG_2090_replaced([11112612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX14_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Selection of the second best beams if only one beam is reported (5G_UP_ALG_2092_replaced([11112621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX15fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * The best and the second best beam selection in UL subcell with 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (5G_UP_ALG_2094_replaced([11112627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX15_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Trigger for beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2068_replaced([11112639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX16vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * Exception for beam sweeping for long PUCCH and UCA (5G_UP_ALG_2097_replaced([11112645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX17PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



ILLA and OLLA updates during beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_2100_replaced([11112657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-2 UL beam sweeping Order of beam sweeping. (ID: 11112539)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11112546`)

UL beam sweeping Triggered as described in 5G_UP_ALG_509_replaced([11098979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knBskPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-PS shall sweep the candidate beam set which consists of SSB beam Ids in the order from 0 to the value of [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] (NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks) [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001].

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-3 UL beam sweeping Rate of beam sweeping. (ID: 11112549)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11112553`)

UL beam sweeping The SSB beam sweeping as triggered by 5G_UP_ALG_2068_replaced([11112639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpX16vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be conducted in UL slots where a given UE is scheduled anyway with period = beam report periodicity as a maximum sweeping rate, which is relevant if the UE is often scheduled. The minimum sweeping rate, which is relevant if the UE is rarely scheduled, is defined by the parameter rdNumSweepingSlotVsNumNonSweepingUlSlot (5G_L2_1242_replaced([11183647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMh_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is the ratio of sweeping slots versus non-sweeping UL slots.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-4 UL beam sweeping Channels measured for  beam sweeping. (ID: 11112558)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11112564`)

UL beam sweeping In each period of beam sweeping as triggered by 5G_UP_ALG_509_replaced([11098979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knBskPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) the candidate SSB beam shall be applied to each UL channels PUSCH, PUCCH F2 [Before CNI-83410] or F3 [End CNI-83410] beam report, PUCCH F2 [Before CNI-83410] or F3 [End CNI-83410] CSI AQC report once.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-5 UL beam sweeping Method of measurement for beam sweeping. (ID: 11112568)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11112572`)

UL beam sweeping 5G-L2-PS shall measure SINR on PUSCH as in 5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and compare SINR values normalized by the number of PRBs as in 5G_UP_ALG_2048_replaced([11112469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Once a candidate beam was measured, the next beam of the candidate set except the beams considered as muted as per 5G_UP_ALG_2240_replaced([11113816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpejkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used in the next sweeping period.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-6 UL beam sweeping Application of the beam sweeping measurements outcome to UL channels and signals. (ID: 11112575)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11112581`)

UL beam sweeping If the condition in 5G_UP_ALG_2102_replaced([11112666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met, 5G-L2-PS shall use the beam with highest measured SINR as the serving UL beam for PUSCH, PUCCH with HARQ feedback and CSI reports, and AP-SRS in UL slots which are NOT sweeping slots.

Note: behavior for dlMimoMode CL8x4MIMO is provided in the 5G_UP_ALG_2062_replaced([11112532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWn0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-7 UL beam sweeping Application of the beam sweeping measurements outcome to DL channels and signals. (ID: 11112583)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11112586`)

UL beam sweeping If the condition in 5G_UP_ALG_2102_replaced([11112666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met, 5G-L2-PS shall use the beam with highest measured SINR as the serving DL beam for PDCCH, PDSCH, CSI-RS (CSI) ACQ.

Note 1: CP3 requirement how 2nd DL beam is defined.

Note: If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO, first and second PMI beam saved in DL UE context shall not updated based on UL beam sweeping result. PDCCH/PDSCH shall only use this SSB beam ID output by beam sweeping when CSI feedback is out of date as defined by 5G_UP_ALG_3188_replaced([11139322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-8 UL beam sweeping Stopping beam sweeping. (ID: 11112591)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11112594`)

UL beam sweeping 5G-L2-PS shall update the 1st serving DL beam except the beams considered as muted as per 5G_UP_ALG_2240_replaced([11113816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpejkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PDSCH until the first CSI report for BM is received or in appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): if the condition in 5G_UP_ALG_2102_replaced([11112666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met . If an CSI report for BM is received and if this UCI meets condition in 5G_UP_ALG_1992_replaced([11112073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) that it can trigger a beam change , 5G-L2-PS shall stop beam sweeping and notify DL scheduler with new target beam. 5G_L2-PS shall update above UL - and DL serving beam in the UE context. 

Example: For above beam solution, the DL and UL beam sequence is as follows assuming beamId#1 is used at the beginning, and only beamId#3 SINR is better, rdUlBeamSweepingTriggerCounts=3), and if appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) : the condition in 5G_UP_ALG_2102_replaced([11112666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met:

DL(PDSCH):

1111111111111111113333333333333333333…3333

DL(CSI report) PUCCH F2 for BM and for LA:

1__1__1__0__1__2__3__4__5__0__1__2__3…3__3

UL(PUSCH)

1111111110111112113334335330331332333…3333

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-9 UL beam sweeping Skipping  UL fallback function upon triggering of  beam sweeping. (ID: 11112599)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11112602`)

UL beam sweeping If beam sweeping is started as described in 5G_UP_ALG_509_replaced([11098979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knBskPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall stop UL fallback function (5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if applicable.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-10 UL beam sweeping Resuming UL fallback function upon finishing the  beam sweeping. (ID: 11112606)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11112609`)

UL beam sweeping If beam sweeping has stopped as described 5G_UP_ALG_509_replaced([11098979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knBskPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS shall again consider trigger conditions of UL fallback function (5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if applicable.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-11 UL beam sweeping Difference between the best and the second best beam. (ID: 11112612)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11112617`)

UL beam sweeping If a second best beam is used in DL, 5G-L2-PS must not apply the same beam Id as first beam and second beam.

Note: If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO, UL beam sweeping related function is not changed.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-12 UL beam sweeping Selection of the second best beams if only one beam is reported. (ID: 11112621)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11112623`)

UL beam sweeping When

a) dlMimoMode "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" or "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO" (values 1,3) and

b) the UE only reports one beam (nrOfReportedRS = n1 in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2684_replaced([11303281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqj_0PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and

c) and beam refinement is disabled, the behavior shall be as follow: 

random beam Id different from the Id of the best beam shall be used for the second best beam.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-13 UL beam sweeping The best and the second best beam selection in subcells with 4 or 8 spatial streams (ID: 11112627)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `11112635`)

UL beam sweeping If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given ul subcell(5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), beam sweeping described in this requirement shall be conducted by keeping old first best UL beam while sweep UL SSB beam as second UL beam, where old first beam UL beam means the first best UL beam recorded in UE database when beam sweeping is triggered, or the new selected DL serving beam if 5G_UP_ALG_2102_replaced([11112666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) criteria is met. Beam specific SINR(5G_UP_ALG_2049_replaced([11112474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWAvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used to determine the swept SSB beam. If during beam sweeping a candidate beam (as second UL beam) is as same as first UL beam, then 5G-L2-PS shall skip this candidate beam by select next candidate beam for sweeping; The skipped candidate beam shall be still be kept in candidate beam set since the first UL beam might be changed during beam sweeping due to serving beam update (in such case 5G-L2-PS may need skip another candidate beam in next round sweeping if the sweeping exit criteria is not yet met).

If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given ul subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the serving UL beam means the first best UL beam, while the 2nd best UL beam selection is determined by CP3.

[Before CNI-83410] If additionally, only 1 SSB beam used for reception of PUCCH Format 3 (when the 2nd reception beam is the full-sector beam, as per 5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the first best beam is not kept (first beam is being swept), and the 2nd beam remains the full-sector beam.

[End CNI-83410]

Note. For Long PUCCH, beam sweeping is disabled appliedUlBeamSweeping is set to FALSE.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-14 UL beam sweeping Trigger for beam sweeping. (ID: 11112639)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11112643`)

UL beam sweeping In appliedUlBeamSweeping == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If CSI report for beam management is DTX’ed (5G_UP_ALG_22403_replaced([11187538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbanvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and/or its CRC failed continuously for more than rdUlBeamSweepingTriggerCounts (5G_L2_1241_replaced([11183642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMhvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UE is considered as beam lost. If so, 5G-L2-PS shall conduct SSB beam sweeping until a target beam is able to receive the CSI report for beam management in a NON-DTX’ed manner.

For UEs which are configured with periodic SRS and state machine for BM is NOT under the state of SRS_BM_AGED (see 5G_UP_ALG_2136_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UL beam sweeping shall NOT be triggered because UL beams are selected based on periodic SRS but not on beam reports from UEs.

If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UE is configured with 2 SSB beams and beam refinement is disabled for the UE and periodic SRS is not configured for the UE, UL beam sweeping shall not be triggered.

For FR1 SCell with UL configured according to 5G_UP_ALG_2698_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), UL beam sweeping shall not be triggered. Note: SCell beam report over PUCCH will be over PCell only, also SCell will be released at bad radio link condition based on measurement after it is configured.

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-15 UL beam sweeping Exception for beam sweeping for long PUCCH and UCA (ID: 11112645)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `11112654`)

UL beam sweeping [Before CNI-83410]

For Long PUCCH, when PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), DTX'ed beam report shall trigger UL beam sweeping.

For Long PUCCH, when PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is disabled (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), DTX'ed beam report shall NOT trigger UL beam sweeping, as the Long PUCCH is received by sector beam (as per CB006064-D).

Note For Long PUCCH, beam sweeping is disabled appliedUlBeamSweeping is set to FALSE.

Note: In case of UCA cell (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1-TDD, eCPRI, UL subcell with 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , appliedUlBeamSweeping shall be FALSE, and UL beam selection is performed according to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and does not rely on beam report.

[End CNI-83410]

---

##### 3.2.6.8.1.0-16 UL beam sweeping ILLA and OLLA updates during beam sweeping. (ID: 11112657)

**3.2.6.8.1.0-16.0-1**  (ID: `11112661`)

UL beam sweeping UL slots used for sweeping are not considered by to OLLA and ILLA, see 5G_UP_ALG_3078_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3060_replaced([11129299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq78IPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 5G_UP_ALG_3153_replaced([11137866](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krcScfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: Proposal for further development, also consider PUCCH F2 SINR / RSRP measurements especially if PUSCH allocations are rare.

### 3.2.6.9 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE

#### 3.2.6.9.0-1 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE UE configuration state and TCI State indication (ID: 12792669)

**3.2.6.9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13431540`)

TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE While the UE dedicated configuration is not activated in the UE side, the gNB must not send any TCI update indication to the UE.  
The UE dedicated configuration state is activated just before the completion of the RRC Setup or RRC Resume or RRC reestablishment procedures according to the content of the message sent (see [11153286: DL-CCCH and DL-DCCH management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

When the U-Plane considers that the UE dedicated configuration is activated, the U-Plane has to send a TCI update indication for all CORESETs configured in the UE including the CORESET(0):

· When there is a beam change triggered by the gNB, or 

· When there is a beam change triggered by the UE through a RA procedure ([11153186: TCI update for UE according to dedicated configuration state](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksk64PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), or 

· When the C-Plane updates the UE configuration about the CORESETs.

[04967706-25R3] ; When the UE dedicated configuration is not yet activated ([11153286: DL-CCCH and DL-DCCH management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), only one CORESET is configured (associated to the Type1 PDCCH) and no TCI are configured yet. Therefore, during this phase, if the UE triggers a Random Access (RA) procedure ([11152251: Random Access Procedures (CBRA/CFRA)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kse0SfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) on a different SS/PBCH compared to the one used before the RA procedure, the U-Plane considers that the Beam Failure Recovery (BFR) is completed and successful without any TCI update and uses this new beam for any new transmission, even if the RA procedure was triggered by the UE for another reason (Uplink data arrival without Scheduling Request (SR) configured yet). [End 04967706-25R3]

---

#### 3.2.6.9.0-2 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE (ID: 11112678)

**3.2.6.9.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `12578012`)

TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE If a new target SSB beam is selected for the UE caused by either the SSB index changes or the related SSB index of a refined beam changes, see 5G_UP_ALG_1937_replaced([11111754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), a TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE shall be sent and the UE shall be eligible for DL scheduling [5G_UP_ALG_18928_replaced([11174508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]. The value of the MAC CE parameter "TCI State ID" = _SSB Index of the target (related) SSB beam. Other unchanged MAC CE parameter values for_

_Serving Cell ID = sCellIndex [5G_CP_ARC_ALG_940_replaced([11245482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tm-gYPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] _,**

and _CORESET ID = value defined in 5G_L2_837_replaced([11173906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26fnYfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._

If a UE is configured to several coresets per cell with Id larger than the value zero (as received at user setup or user modify), 5G-L2-PS shall signal the TCI state as defined in [5G_UP_ALG_8673_replaced([11112728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

For FR1 CA **UE with TDD Scell beamforming activated, Scell TCI state indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE shall be sent over Scell or over PCell, cf. 5G_UP_ALG_2108_replaced([11112694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

In _appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):_

If PUCCH F2 or F3 SINR for beam report < rdThresholdUlProbingBeforeDlBeamChange (5G_L2_1245_replaced([11183687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lMjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and Long PUCCH UCI does not arrive over PUSCH, and if a new target SSBbeam is selected for the UE caused either the SSB index changes or the related SSB index of a refined beam changes, see 5G_UP_ALG_1937_replaced([11111754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), an updated beam ID shall be applied first in UL PUSCH, see 5G_UP_ALG_2056_replaced([11112507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If condition in 5G_UP_ALG_2056_replaced([11112507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is met, a TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE shall be sent and the UE shall be eligible for DL scheduling [5G_UP_ALG_18928_replaced([11174508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

**NOTE: This 5G19A Pronto should not be applicable if pure SRS based beam selection is conducted such as in 5G19B 5GC001258.**

5G-L2-PS shall execute TCI state signaling while beam toggling as defined in [5G_UP_ALG_7972_replaced([11112714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYdAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

If supercell mode is enabled **[CB009543-B] in TDD**[End CB009543-B], refer to 5G-UP_5471, 5G-L2-PS shall execute TCI state signalling, due to subcell switch, refer to 5G_UP_5553_replaced([11353464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub_hXvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).****

Additional MAC CEs for PDCCH TCI State Indication are sent, see 5G_UP_ALG_2111_replaced([11112722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **A** MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication (5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2111_replaced([11112722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be sent before the previous MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication for the same component carrier is completed. That means the transport block containing the previous MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication for the same component carrier is HARQ ACKed or finally HARQ NACKed**.** ****

If _beamGroupSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 1, MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication shall be not sent if the target beam is not RRC configured to the UE, that is not in the active beam group see 5G_UP_ALG_2227_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._

**NOTE:**

· TCI State of the PDSCH is implicitly signaled by PDCCH TCI state indication, since the parameter _tci-PresentInDCI = disabled (, i.e., the parameter is omitted) in PDCCH-Config in a hardcoded manner as defined by 5GC000533-BC in 5G_CP_IF_RRC_2125_replaced([11333028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wU-RqvvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Only for information, if by a later feature this flag is enabled, then PDSCH is not directly QCL binded to PDCCH but needs own beam indication by MAC-CE and DCI._

· For FR1, more than number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) TCI-States may be defined, e.g., to be referenced in CSI-RS for tracking. It has to be ensured that the TCI-States valid for being referenced in PDCCH start with 0 and have all the same Id as the related SSB beam; in case of CSI-RS for tracking, the TCI-State linked to these CSI-RS must refer to the SS/PBCH block with the same ID as the hosting TCI-State: CSI-RS-for-tracking -> TCI-State -> TCI-StateId = CSI-RS-for-tracking -> TCI-State -> QCL-Info -> ssb.

#### 3.2.6.9.0-3 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE with multiple active component carriers (ID: 11112694)

**3.2.6.9.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `13480958`)

TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE [Before CB013712-B] on FR2, in the case UE has more than one active component carrier when a new target beam is selected as per 5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), one TCI state indication MAC CE shall be sent for each active component carrier using the same transport block.

On FR2, TCI State ID shall be configured identically for all MAC CE. Serving Cell ID, BWP ID and CORESET ID shall be set according to each component carrier configuration.[End CB013712-B] 

For FDD + FR1 TDD CA, target beam selection is only be valid for TDD Scell so TCI state indication shall only be send to Scell through MAC CE according to 5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**For FR1 CA, TCI state indication shall be send to each carrier separately through MAC CE according to 5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

The very first PDSCH transmission on SCell shall be the TCI state indication on the best SSB beam reported to PCell in the first CSI report after Scell Activation CE. For FR1 TDD SCell with UL CA configured and supercell mode enabled or a TDD supercell SCell with an FDD supercell PCell, the very first PDSCH transmission on the SCell shall be the TCI state indication on the SCell target beam (see 5G_UP_ALG_2017_replaced([11112151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after SCell activation.

NOTE**: For** FR1 CA with SCell NRBTS/NRCELL/actBeamforming = false, if SCell status is changed to active, if CoreSet-Id is configured equal 0 in UE-specific Search Space of active BWP, a MAC CE for PDCCH TCI state indication is sent, as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2804_replaced([11121880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqa-y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).****

Note: for IODT with QualComm UE, sending the first TCI indication MAC CE as the very first PDSCH transmission on Scell on the best SSB beam reported to PCell in the first CSI report after Scell Activation CE is sufficient, because QualComm has confirmed that their UE will expect the transmission on the best SSB beam if no TCI activation MAC CE has been recieved by the UE**.**

For FR1 TDD as Scell with BF activated, the order of operation wrt. TCI state indication for the SCell shall be as follows:

  1. After receiving HARQ Ack for Scell activation MAC CE, P(S)Cell waits for the first CSI report for beam managament.

  2. As soon as the beam report has been received, PCell passes the report to Scell.

  3. SCell deduces from the report the TCI state indication MAC CE content for the best beam received, and passes this TCI state indication content to the PCell.

  4. PCell transmits the TCI state indication MAC CE to the UE.

  5. After receiving the HARQ Ack for the TCI state indication MAC CE, PCell indicates to Scell to start the normal mode of beamforming operation.

  6. As long as Scell reports CQI > 0 (so no overheating and no beam failure aka virtual RLF), the subsequent TCI state indication MAC CEs can be sent on Scell or on PCell - this is left to CP3 decision.

  7. If Scell reports CQI=0, then this is an indication that either the UE is in overheating state or the Ue has lost the beam (vRLF). The same handling is applied during scheduling suspend due to bad RLQ. At beam change, PCell sends a TCI state indication.




Note: Although the UE is not scheduled on Scell, it still measures the SSB and CSI-RS and provides CSI reports on Scell.

  1. As soon as gNB receives reliable CQI>0, because either UE was configured with the correct beam or it cooled down,or because bad RLQ condition has vanished, the Scell can resume PDSCH transmission on the new beam as soon as TCI activation CA ack has been passed from the PCell.



For FR1 FDD as Scell with BF activated, the order of operation wrt. TCI state indication for the SCell shall be as follows:

  1. After receiving HARQ Ack for Scell activation MAC CE, P(S)Cell shall wait for the first CSI report for channel acquisition.

  2. As soon as the CSI report has been received, PCell passes the report to Scell.

  3. gNB transmits the TCI state indication MAC CE to the UE. Note only one SSB is available for FDD.

  4. After receiving the HARQ Ack for the TCI state indication MAC CE, PCell indicates to Scell to start the normal mode of beamforming operation.

  5. If Scell reports CQI=0, then this is an indication that either the UE is in overheating state or the Ue has lost the beam (vRLF). The same handling is applied during scheduling suspend due to bad RLQ. 

  6. As soon as gNB receives reliable CQI>0, because either UE was configured with the correct beam or it cooled down,or because bad RLQ condition has vanished, the Scell can resume PDSCH transmission without new TCI state indication since there is no SSB beam change.




Note: Although the UE is not scheduled on Scell, it still measures the SSB and CSI-RS and provides CSI reports on Scell.

---

#### 3.2.6.9.0-4 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE TCI State Signalling while Beam Toggling (ID: 11112714)

**3.2.6.9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11112717`)

TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE In appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange == TRUE (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If for a given user two (x-pol.) beams are applied for a DL transmission, and only the order of 1st beam Id and 2nd beam Id changes, so that old 1st beam becomes new 2nd beam and old 2nd beam becomes new 1st beam, 5G-L2-PS MAC CE shall not send a TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE. The TCI state of the best beam shall be signaled, if the configured TCI state does not correspond two any of the two best (target) beams.

If NRBTS-actBeamControlImprovement1 == TRUE:

The TCI state of the best beam ID = i shall be signaled, if the filtered power value of beam ID = i is larger than the source beam (configured TCI state) value plus an offset value [5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced([11112105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] and an additional offset value defined by the parameter rdBeamTogglingAddPowerOffset_dB [5G_UP_ALG_7970_replaced([11113972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

That is if this condition is met: filteredReceivePower_dBm[beam ID = i] > filteredReceivePower_dBm[source beam] + rdBeamMgmtPowerOffset_dB + rdBeamTogglingAddPowerOffset_dB.

NOTE: Skipping signaling beam order changes avoids UE loops reset and corresponding performance losses.

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO, and appliedDlBeamProbingBeforeChange= TRUE :

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2056_replaced([11112507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.2.6.9.0-5 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE Additional TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE (ID: 11112722)

**3.2.6.9.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `13480962`)

TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE 5G-L2-PS shall send additional MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication, if the UE is eligible for DL scheduling in [5G_UP_ALG_4183_replaced([11174302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuat9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] in following cases

· If 5G-LS-PS applies the new 1st beam after a beam change the first time to PDSCH [5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

· If the beam was reported _N times since the last sent MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indication, where_ N = _rdAdditionalBeamIndMacCePeriod [5G_L2_1270_replaced([11183744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27lzmvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]. [Before CB013712-B] In FR2 ([11346889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubH-rPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-LS-PS shall cease the periodic transmission of MAC CE PDCCH TCI state indications after four occurrences following a beam change ([11112294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUyl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or a beam failure recovery random access procedure ([11369402](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udqVRvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB013712-B]_**

· After a beam failure recovery triggered by the UE with a Random Access procedure on another SS/PBCH (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_22395_replaced([11174363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

· If 5G-L2-PS has successfully switched to a BWP in which CORESET Id equal 0 is configured in USS (5G_UP_ALG_1857_replaced([11111082](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpKagvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**. NOTE: that is a network workaround for a UE bug, which is needed if the USS is configured with coreset Id equal 0.**

· When the C-Plane changes the mapping between cell BWP and the UE BWP or when a BWP is added in the UE and not when the inactive BWP is released, on the serving cell with a DL-DCCH[RRC reconfiguration, resume or reestablishment] or DL-CCCH[RRC setup], the U-Plane has to send MAC Control Element TCI state indication on all CORESETs defined in the set of BWPs (included CORESET(0) if associated to a search space (common or UE-Specific)) configured in the UE with the RRC message.

The active TCI state of the PDCCH DMRS shall be used in the additional MAC CE.

5G-L2-PS shall prioritize MAC CEs as defined in [5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] over additional MAC CEs as defined in this requirement

beam report counter is not increased when UE in overheating or bad RLQ.

In FR1 CA, when UE is in bad RLQ or in overheating/vRLF, the UE is not scheduled on Scell. The beam report counter keeps increasing, but because the UE is not scheduled on Scell, the TCI state Indication is not to be sent. The additional TCI state can be sent only as soon as UE can be scheduled on Scell, however, only the newest TCI state should be sent, the previous ones are discarded.

---

#### 3.2.6.9.0-6 TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE TCI State Signaling with several dedicated BWPs configured per UE (ID: 11112728)

**3.2.6.9.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12527409`)

TCI State Indication for UE-specific PDCCH MAC CE [Before PR825516-25R2]If a UE is configured to several coresets per cell with Id larger than the value zero (as received at user setup or user modify) when a new target beam is selected as per 5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), one TCI state indication MAC CE shall be sent for each configured coreset with Id larger than the value zero, using the same transport block. 5G-L2-PS shall also consider coresets Ids from inactive BWPs.

[PR825516-25R2]In case of user setup or user modify, TCI update triggering and content are described in [11112722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End PR825516-25R2]

## 3.2.7 Beam Management

### 3.2.7.0-1 Beam Management Beamforming activation (ID: 11112739)

**3.2.7.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13479167`)

Beam Management If the _NRCELL/actBeamforming is set to_ true, 5G-L2-PS shall use the basic beam set, considering also the beamforming type (see 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and:**

 use the beam IDs according to the selected basic beam set and respective edge angles, see 5G_UP_ALG_11982_replaced([11111700](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This includes also refined beams if present.

 trigger SS block transmission according to the number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 map the beam IDs to the proper pattern IDs, see 5G_UP_ALG_1939_replaced([11111782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If beamforming is disabled for FR1 FDD below 6GHz (with "actBeamforming = False" && "numOfSubSectors = 0"). Therefore, single wide sector-beam is applied and PatternId = 0 shall be used. (indicating that no beamforming is used).

When no beamforming is applied for FR1 TDD below 6GHz (with „actBeamforming = False“ && „numOfSubsectors = 0“), a single wide sector-beam is applied. If a bfSetup is provided by CP-RT, the fullSectorBeampatternId for the full sector beam shall be used (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2480_replaced([11288965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise patternID = 0 (indicating that RF is not BF capable).

_Beamforming is applied for_ FR1 _TDD_ below 6GHz _(with "actBeamforming = True" && "numOfSubSectors = 2 or 4"_). Single SSB beam is applicable in each sub-sector formed by beamforming.***** *

Supercell configuration is applied for FR1 TDD below 6GHz (with "MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actBeamforming = False" and "MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actSupercell = True" and number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch) is greater than 1 (see 5G_UP_83_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). A single SSB beam (virtual SSB beam) is applicable and associated to L1 subcell. For Fronthaul:

 eCPRI the patternId is always set to 0.

Supercell configuration is applied for FDD (with "MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actBeamforming = False" and "MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actSupercell = True" and number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch) is equal to 1 (see 5G_UP_83_replaced([11347173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubKa5_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). A single SSB beam is applicable and associated to all L1 subcells. For Fronthaul:

 eCPRI the patternId is always set to 0.

implement the below request for eCPRI digital beamforming first;implement the below request for CPRI digital beamforming

{

The RU is configured such that the basic beam set #1 with single beam is mapped on patternId = fullSectorBeamPatternId **of bfSetup 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2475_replaced([11288953](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp9i9vvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.****

}

[Before CB013712-B] If _rrmBeamformingType =_ analogBf then SSB configuration _rmAbfSsbConf is always defined by 5G_UP_ALG_1903_replaced([11111484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and _beam ID to _pattern ID mapping is defined by 5G_UP_ALG_1906_replaced([11111517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), in addition to 5G_UP_ALG_11982_replaced([11111700](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB013712-B]_****

If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false [CB008577-B], or dlMimoMode is CL 32x4 MIMO, [End CB008577-B] the number of beams Ntof each configuration set (NBi, N1,N2)t per cell is constructed from two parts, one is the PMI beams for PDSCH/PDCCH (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2506_replaced( 11290062 ) ), the second is the beams for CSI-RS (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2511_replaced( 11290807 )).**** The row x in this requirement refers CSI-RS table in TS38.211. 1) For row 8 (8 ports) CSI-RS transmission: Each direction of a subpanel beam leads to 4 beams for the two symbols of row 8 CSI-RS transmission. The 4 pattern ID of these 4 beams shall be arranged in predefined way. Ascending order for first symbol port 3000, first symbol port 3001, second symbol port 3000, second symbol port 3001. Each direction of subpanel beams leads to 64 2D DFT beams for (N1,N2) = (2,2), 16 DFT beams for (N1,N2) = (4,1). So[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation defines a variable $N_t$ using a piecewise function. The equation is: $N_t = \begin{cases} (N_{Bi} \times (16+4)) &amp; \text{for } (N_1, N_2) = (4,1) \ (N_{Bi} \times (64+4)) &amp; \text{for } (N_1, N_2) = (2,2) \end{cases}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_4934.009.png[/image_path][/image-0] [CB008577-B] 2)For row 6 (8 ports) CSI-RS transmission (only DL direction is needed): 4 beams for the one symbol of CSI-RS. Ascending order for port 3000, 3001, 3002, 3003. Note the other polarization has the same beams but for port 3004, 3005, 3006, 3007. 16 DFT beams for DL channels NBi=1 (N1,N2) = (4,1); [CB008577-C] 16 DFT beams for UL channels.[End CB008577-C] 3) For row 18 (32 ports) CSI-RS transmission: 16 beams for the four symbols of CSI-RS. Each symbol of the four symbols needs 4 beams and they are in ascending order for port 3000, 3001, 3008, 3009. Note the other polarization has the same 4 beams compared to 1st polarization but for port 3016, 3017, 3024, 3025. The other 3 symbols of CSI-RS has different beams compared 1st symbol but beams are arranged in the same order according to ports. For rank1, 2: 256 DFT beams for DL channel for NBi=1, (N1,N2) = (8,2); For rank3, 4: 1024 DFT beams for DL channel for NBi=1, (N1,N2) = (8,2); [End CB008577-B] [CB008577-C] The number of beams for UL channels shall be the number of DFT beam (256 + 1024). Note CSI-RS beams are not needed for UL. [End CB008577-C] Note: This requirement is for PMI beam and not applicable while actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true. (ID: 12765547)

#### 3.2.7.1.1-3 PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports

##### 3.2.7.1.1-3.0-2 PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12806260: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports Below requirement works for when (dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false) [CB008577-B] or dlMimoMode is CL 32x4 [End CB008577-B]. Input: startPatternID [CB008577-B] for 8 ports [End CB008577-B]: the first beam pattern ID that will be used by PMI beams, which will be filled by higher layer. Beam Set list of this time cell set up. Beam Set of PMI beams is described by (NBi, N1,N2)t, refer to ( 11112763 ). Algorithm: Construct PatternID offset (index of PMI beams, startPatternID will be added to it to form the final beam patternID used by RRU): • count DFT beams from PMI first, then subpanel beam from CRI, then 4 beam for CSI-RS added; [CB008577-C] then DFT beam from PMI for UL added [End CB008577-C] ; • inside DFT beams from PMI, count horizontal i1,1 first, then vertical i1,2. • i1,3is not show here, as it refers to beam offset within the same beam candidate set. [Before CB008577-C] patternIdOffset = i x 4 + i x 2biti1,2+ biti1,1 + i1,2x 2biti1,1  + i1,1 + COt. [CB008577-C] patternIdOffset_dl = i x 4 + i x 2biti1,2+ biti1,1 + i1,2x 2biti1,1  + i1,1 + COt. for UL: patternIdOffset_ul = Nt_DL + patternIdOffset_dl where Nt_DL is number of DL DFT beam adding number of CSI-RS beams within the beam set t. [End CB008577-C] i: CRI reported by UE, means subpanel beam index, present if more than one subpanel beams NBi are configured, i is within range [0, NBi - 1]; i1,2 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means vertical direction index, present for N2 &gt; 1, i1,2 is within range [0, N2O2-1]; i1,1 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means horizontal direction index, i1,1 is within range [0, N1O1-1]; biti1,2: number of bits needed for i1,2 subfield; biti1,1 : number of bits needed for i1,1 subfield; COt : index offset of configuration set described by (NBi, N1, N2))t for the cell. t=0 refer to the 1st configuration set for the current cell. Note the number of configuration sets is relevant for RU type, NIDD configuration, for example 8trx RU only have one configuration set, i.e. (N1=4,N2=1, number of subpanel directions is 1). One UE shall be configured with only one beam set at the same time. And COt = 0 for t = 0; COt = COt-1 + Nt-1 ,for t &gt; 0 ; Where Nt-1 is the number of beams for configuration set t-1. The number of beams Nt refer to ( 11112799 ). The 4 CSI-RS beams for each direction of subpanel beams occupy the largest 4 pattern ID within (16+4) or (64+4). Output: Pattern ID of DL [CB008577-C]UL [End CB008577-C] channels used by RU: patternID = patternIdOffset + startPatternID Example of one cell with 64 TRX RUs: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a blurred abstract representation of a logo or graphic element.
