(ID: 12806260)

#### 3.2.7.1.1-4 PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports

##### 3.2.7.1.1-4.0-3 PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports 12765948: PatternID arrangement for PMI beams of different CSI-RS ports Below requirement works for when dlMimoMode is CL 32x4. Input: startPatternID for 32 ports: the first beam pattern ID that will be used by PMI beams based on 32 ports CSI-RS. Note: either cplane directly pass this to L2 or L2 deduce this based on overall PMI beams, left the freedom to CP3 design. Beam Set list of this time cell set up. Beam Set of PMI beams is described by [image-0] image_desc [/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_4936.002.png[/image_path][/image-0], refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2188_replaced( 11112763 ). Number of Beams per Beam Set, refer to 11112799 . Algorithm: Construct PatternID offset as below, which is the index of beams based on 32 ports CSI-RS, startPatternID for 32 ports shall be added to it to form the final beam patternID used by RRU. •       Count DFT beams based on PMI for DL rank1/2 first, beams for DL rank 3/4 in second place, and then beams for CSI-RS transmission. [CB008577-C] PMI beam UL shall be appended after DL. UL PMI beams can be the frequency compensated DL PMI beams except beams for CSI-RS. [End CB008577-C] •       Inside DFT beams based on PMI , count horizontal i1,1 first, vertical i1,2 in second place, and then i1,3 if needed. •       For DL rank1/2: Note:  i1,3is not show here, as it refers to beam offset within the same beam candidate set. For DL: patternIdOffsetr12_DL = i1,2x 2biti1,1  + i1,1 + COt. where i1,2 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means vertical direction index, present for N2 &gt; 1, i1,2 is within range [0, N2O2-1]; i1,1 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means horizontal direction index, i1,1 is within range [0, N1O1-1]; biti1,2 : number of bits needed for i1,2 subfield; biti1,1 : number of bits needed for i1,1 subfield; COt : index offset of configuration set described by (NBi, N1, N2))t for the cell. And COt = 0 for t = 0; COt = COt-1 + Nt-1; •       For rank3/4: patternIdOffsetr34_DL = sign(+-1)x 2biti1,3 + biti1,2 + biti1,1 + i1,3x 2 biti1,2 + biti1,1  + i1,2x 2biti1,1 + i1,1 + Nr12 + COt. sign(1) = 0, sign(-1) = 1, means variety comes from +- Theta_p, and counts all positive Theta_p first, then all  negative Theta_p with larger ID; i1,3 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means variety between each half panel comes from Theta_p, i1,3 has values as 0,1,2,3. i1,2 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means vertical direction index, i1,2 is within range [0, N2O2-1]; i1,1 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means horizontal direction index, high important notify that for rank3/4, i1,1 is within range [0, N1O1/2 - 1]; biti1,3 : number of bits needed for subfield i1,3; biti1,2 : number of bits needed for subfield i1,2; biti1,1 : number of bits needed for subfield i1,1; high important notify that number of bits of i1,1 for rank3/4, is different as i1,1 for rank1/2. •       For CSI-RS transmission: patternIdOffsetCSIRS = CSIRS beam index + Nr34 + Nr12 + COt. where Nr12 is number of beam for rank1/2,  Nr34 is number of beam for rank3/4, refer to 11112799: Beam number for each PMI beam set . [CB008577-C] For UL: patternIdOffset_ul = Nt_DL + patternIdOffset_dl where Nt_DL is number of DL DFT beam adding number of CSI-RS beams within the beam set t. patternIdOffset_DL can be patternIdOffsetr12_DL or patternIdOffsetr34_DL.[End CB008577-C] Overall Pattern ID used by RU is: patternID =patternIdOffset + startPatternID for 32 ports Where patternIdOffset can be patternIdOffsetr12_DL or patternIdOffsetr34_DL or patternIdOffsetCSIRS [CB008577-C] or patternIdOffsetUL[End CB008577-C] mentioned above. Output: Pattern ID used by RU. Note: This requirement is for PMI beam and not applicable while actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true. (ID: 12765948)

### 3.2.7.2 PMI beam change procedure

### 3.2.7.2-1 PMI beam change procedure

#### 3.2.7.2-1.0-2 PMI beam change procedure Some UE's history version does not support LI report and no UE capability to indicate this in RRC signaling. In this case UE fill random bit to LI bit field. If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO [CB008577-B] or 32x4 MIMO, if LI is configured in the CSI report, [End CB008577-B] L2 shall check the LI field and fill mismatched LI field in CSI feedback as 0 for each valid CSI report for channel acquisition. Mismatched LI report is defined as: the indicated layer by LI is larger than rank indicated by RI. [CB008577-B] If dlMimoMode is 32x4 MIMO, if LI is NOT configured in the CSI report, L2 shall and fill LI field in CSI feedback as 0 for each valid CSI report for channel acquisition. Rationale: to prepare later solutions that LI is not needed depending on best PMI beam is needed or not, cplane support not configure LI but L2 has not been ready for switch beam type used by each channel. [End CB008577-B] Note: For UEs not support LI report, PMI beam is still trusted and used in DL, so if actDlMuMimo is enabled and port selection for rank 2 is needed, the best PMI beam shall still be used with assumption that LI = 0. (ID: 12828626)

#### 3.2.7.2.0-1 PMI beam change procedure PMI beam change procedure based on 8 ports CSI-RS (ID: 11112965)

**3.2.7.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12806258`)

PMI beam change procedure Input:

startPatternID for PMI beams of DL [CB008577-C] and optional UL. [End CB008577-C];

COt : index offset of configuration set described by (NBi, N1, N2))t for the cell.

UCI in CSI feedback, which include:

i : CRI reported by UE, means subpanel beam index, present if more than one CSI-RS resources within the CSI-RS resource set are configured;

i1,2 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means vertical direction index, present for N2 > 1, i1,2 is within range [0, N2O2-1];

i1,1 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means horizontal direction index, i1,1 is within range [0, N1O1-1];

i1,3: subfield of PMI reported by UE, for rank1/2, it means offset of the two PMI beams; for rank3/4, it means half panel shifter.

LI: Layer Indicator reported by UE, means which column of the precoding matrix is the strongest.

Algorithm:

[CB008577-C] For DL:[End CB008577-C]

Find 1st beam pattern ID:

patternIdOffset = i x 4 + i x 2biti1,2+ biti1,1 + i1,2x 2biti1,1 + i1,1 + COt.

Find 2nd beam pattern ID:

For Rank1, the 2nd beam pattern ID is the same as the 1st .

For Rank2: Using i1,3 to get: (i1,2+ k2)mod (N2 O2), (i1,1+ k1)mod (N1 O1), where k1 and k2 are defined by TS38.214 Table 5.2.2.2.1-3 and Table 5.2.2.2.1-4.

patternIdOffset = i x 4 + i x 2biti1,2+ biti1,1 + {(i1,2+ k2)mod (N2 O2)} x 2biti1,1 + {(i1,1+ k1)mod (N1 O1)} + COt.

Find the best beam of the two via LI if two different beams are reported:

|  |   
---|---|---  
1 bit LI | 2 bit LI | Best beam  
0 | 00 | 1st  
1 | 01 | 2nd  
| 10 | 1st  
| 11 | 2nd  
  
[CB008577-C] For UL: patternIdOffset_ul = Nt_DL + patternIdOffset_dl, where patternIdOffset_dl is patternIdOffset for DL above, Nt_DL refers to: [11112829: PatternIDs for PMI beams based on 8 ports CSI-RS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). UL best PMI beam shall be the one mapped by DL best PMI beam, UL second best PMI beam shall be the one mapped by DL second best PMI beam. [End CB008577-C]

Find PatternID used by RU by add startPatternID to patternIdOffset. where patternIdOffset can be patternIdOffset, patternIdOffset_ul above.

Output:

The PatternIDs of two beams and best one of the two for this UE for DL [CB008577-C] and UL. [End CB008577-C] scheduling.

NOTE: Due to TD scheduler limit rrmMaxNumBeamsDStream for FD scheduling(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4478_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the beam that'll be used for PDSCH/PDCCH transmission in that symbol shall be used for checking UE's DL beam. This is valid for both initial transmission and retransmission. So if dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO, either PMI beam or SSB beam can be used for PDSCH/PDSCH transmission.

Note: 1st and 2nd pattern ID shall be used for PDSCH transmission with the order of original report, instead of feeding the best beam for the 1st PDSCH stream. Rational is the beam weight has part of precoding included and all precoding are aligned with CSI feedback by UE.

---

#### 3.2.7.2.0-2 PMI beam change procedure PMI beam change procedure based on 32 ports CSI-RS (ID: 12806255)

**3.2.7.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12806256`)

PMI beam change procedure Input:

startPatternID for PMI beams of DL [CB008577-C] and UL. [End CB008577-C];

COt : index offset of configuration set described by (NBi, N1, N2))t for the cell.

UCI in CSI feedback, which include:

i1,2 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means vertical direction index, present for N2 > 1, i1,2 is within range [0, N2O2-1];

i1,1 : subfield of PMI reported by UE, means horizontal direction index, i1,1 is within range [0, N1O1-1];

COt : index offset of configuration set described by (NBi, N1, N2))t for the cell. And

i1,3: subfield of PMI reported by UE, for rank1/2, it means offset of the two PMI beams; for rank3/4, it means half panel shifter.

LI: Layer Indicator reported by UE, means which column of the precoding matrix is the strongest.

Algorithm:

If Rank1 and Rank2,

Find 1st beam pattern ID:

patternIdOffsetr12 = i1,2x 2biti1,1 + i1,1 + COt.

Find 2nd beam pattern ID:

For Rank 1: the 2nd beam pattern ID is the same as the 1st beam.

For Rank2: Using i1,3 to get: (i1,2+ k2)mod (N2 O2), (i1,1+ k1)mod (N1 O1), where k1 and k2 are defined by TS38.214 Table 5.2.2.2.1-3.

patternIdOffsetr12 = {(i1,2+ k2)mod (N2 O2)} x 2biti1,1 + {(i1,1+ k1)mod (N1 O1)} + COt.

If Rank 3 and Rank4:

Find 1st beam pattern ID:

patternIdOffsetr34 =

i1,3x 2 biti1,2 + biti1,1 + i1,2x 2biti1,1 + i1,1 + Nr12 + COt.

Find 2nd beam pattern ID:

patternIdOffsetr34 =

2biti1,3 + biti1,2 + biti1,1 + i1,3x 2 biti1,2 + biti1,1 + i1,2x 2biti1,1 + i1,1 + Nr12 + COt.

Find the best beam of the two via LI if two different beams are reported:

|  |   
---|---|---  
1 bit LI | 2 bit LI | Best beam  
0 | 00 | 1st  
1 | 01 | 2nd  
| 10 | 1st  
| 11 | 2nd  
  
[CB008577-C] For UL: patternIdOffset_ul = Nt_DL + patternIdOffset_dl, where patternIdOffset_dl can be patternIdOffsetr12, patternIdOffsetr34above. Nt_DL refers to: [11112950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). UL best PMI beam shall be the one mapped by DL best PMI beam, UL second best PMI beam shall be the one mapped by DL second best PMI beam. [End CB008577-C]

Find PatternID used by RU by add startPatternID to patternIdOffset. where patternIdOffset can be patternIdOffsetr12, patternIdOffsetr34, patternIdOffset_ul above.

Output:

The PatternIDs of two beams and best one of the two for this UE for DL [CB008577-C] and UL. [End CB008577-C] scheduling.

Note: 1st and 2nd pattern ID shall be used for PDSCH transmission with the order of original report, instead of feeding the best beam for the 1st PDSCH stream. Rational is the beam weight has part of precoding included and all precoding are aligned with CSI feedback by UE.

---

#### 3.2.7.2.0-3 PMI beam change procedure PUCCH SINR check for CSI feedback (ID: 11112082)

**3.2.7.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12828628`)

PMI beam change procedure If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4MIMO [CB008577-D] 32x4MIMO [End CB008577-D] in PCell or SCell then for UEs with 8[CB008577-D] /32 [End CB008577-D] ports CSI-RS configured:

L2 discards DTX'ed CSI reports received via Format 2 or Format 3 **and not use CRI, RI, LI, PMI, CQI of this report.**

**False CRC ok protection:**

If 1) a CSI feedback is nonDTX'ed and has an instantaneous SINR value (5G_UP_ALG_3623_replaced([11160031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < _rdThresholdUciBm_dB ([11191901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28gZlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 2) report payload received over Format 3 is less than 20bit (6bit CRC length) and UCI does not arrive over PUSCH,_

\- if the next UCI for CSI feedback is nonDTX'ed and includes the similar PMI beams as the one before (including the one that is treated as invalid by this requirement),

The report shall be handled as valid. Note the report is still saved as temporary info and is used to decide when the next report is trustworthy or not.

\- else

The report shall be handled as invalid.

else

The report shall be handled as valid.

L2 shall update the PMI beam, PMI, RI, LI and CQI info from valid report for the UE context in corresponding serving cell , see 5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008577-D] If dlMimoMode is CL 8x4: [End CB008577-D] Similar PMI beams here means the mapped SSB beam for twice PMI feedback is the same. PMI and SSB beam mapping refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2517_replaced([11294511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqDplvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008577-D] If dlMimoMode is CL 32x4: similar PMI beams shall be: i11, i12 are not changed larger than 3 steps for twice PMI feedback. For i11 of 32 ports rank3/4 shall be mapped to i11 of rank1/2 by multiply 2 for comparation. Note i13 is not used for simplification. In scenarios where bit length of i11,i12 are changed, this verification checking can be simplified by implementation. E.g. absolute value of (latest i11 - previous i11) = 3 is seen as 3 steps. [End CB008577-D]

**Note: above description shall also be applicable when actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 4 **or 6, in which case**L2 PS still use PMI beam. The PMI beam pattern ID maps to SSB beam ID refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9731_replaced([11113316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) while actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true.******

Note: Harq and SR that possibly multiplexed with this CSI feedback is not impacted here, L2 use any feedback L1 reported.

Note: legacy CQI check in 5G_UP_ALG_4620_replaced([11187546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvcBofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is handled in parallel.

Note:

[Before CB008577-D]1. For FR1 TDD CA UE, if Pcell has dlMimoMode other than CL 8x4MIMO but Scell has dlMimoMode with CL 8x4MIMO, above procedure shall still be performed for Scell.

[CB008577-D] For CA cases, if Pcell has dlMimoMode other than CL 8x4/32x4 but Scell has dlMimoMode with CL 8x4/32x4, above procedure shall still be performed for Scell. [End CB008577-D]

---

### 3.2.7.3 SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell

#### 3.2.7.3.0-1 SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell Beam ID specification in UCA Cell (ID: 11113032)

**3.2.7.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11113039`)

SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell Uniform Circular Array (UCA) cell (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall obtain DL SSB beams with the number equal to [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] NRCELL.numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001], and fixedly 2 UL beams.

The sequential pattern IDs of DL SSB beams and selected UL beams are respectively delivered in the interface (reference to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2476_replaced([11288959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

These pattern IDs of beam weights and their orders shall be the input of beam control algorithm in UCA cell scenario. The algorithm can reference to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL beam and 5G_UP_ALG_2210_replaced([11113043](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL beam.

Uniform Circular Array (UCA) cell (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall obtain DL SSB beams with the number equal to [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] and fixedly 2 UL beams.

The sequential pattern IDs of DL SSB beams [CB008285-E-UPD001] (activated SS/PBCH) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] and selected UL beams are respectively delivered in the interface (reference to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2476_replaced([11288959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

These pattern IDs of beam weights and their orders shall be the input of beam control algorithm in UCA cell scenario. The algorithm can reference to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL beam and 5G_UP_ALG_2210_replaced([11113043](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL beam.

#### 3.2.7.3.0-2 SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell SSB beam weight configuration for UCA cell (ID: 11113043)

**3.2.7.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11113050`)

SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell In case of UCA cell scenario (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

DL SSB beam weights for UCA cell shall be sequentially input via interface(reference to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2476_replaced([11288959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Their number shall be equal to [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] NRCELL.numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001].

The inputted DL SSB beam weights shall be sequentially mapped to [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] SS/PBCH Block Index [CB008285-E-UPD001] index of activated SS/PBCH list (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001], as legacy SSB beamforming procedure in 5G_UP_ALG_1940_replaced([11111787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The precoder setting for 8TX transmissions in UCA cell is same to legacy procedure defined as 5G_UP_ALG_3188_replaced([11139322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3185_replaced([11139392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmqi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.2.7.3.0-3 SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell Fixed configuration of beam weights for Uplink reception in UCA cell (ID: 11113055)

**3.2.7.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11113058`)

SSB beam and UL beam management for UCA cell In case of omni UCA cell scenario (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), uplink channels, PUXCH,SRS and PRACH and UL channels shall be fixedly configured with 4RX with beam weight according to 5G_UP_933_replaced([11353761](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucB9l_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Each two consecutive eAxCs, which separately map to different polarities of RFU TRX groups, shall use the same pattern ID of beam weight.

Thus, 2 UL beam weights shall be required for all UL channels to configure 4RX in UCA cell.

  * for PRACH related to random access procedure, the first pattern ID fixedly map to first two streams, and the second pattern ID fixedly map to the the second two streams, please reference to 5G_L2_467_replaced([11178972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27DBDfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PRACH related beam ID scheduling in UCA.
  * for MSG3 within PUSCH related to random access procedure, the first pattern ID fixedly map to first two streams, and the second pattern ID fixedly map to the second two streams, please reference to 5G_L2_467_replaced([11178972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27DBDfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for MSG3 within PUSCH related beam ID scheduling in UCA, 5G_L2_899_replaced([11179052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27DoHPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for MSG3 related beam ID configuration.
  * same beam weight configuration is configured for PUSCH and PUCCH related to UE in RRC connection, i.e. the first pattern ID fixedly map to first two streams, and the second pattern ID fixedly map to the second two streams, please reference to 5G_L2_467_replaced([11178972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27DBDfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUSCH related beam ID scheduling in UCA.
  * Especially for long PUCCH case, in case of UCA cell scenario, same two UL beams are fixedly used as other UL channels, instead of sector beams. (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2476_replaced([11288959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).



Fixed 2 UL beam weights shall be configured during UCA cell working, and UL beam selection does not rely on beam report. Those legacy UL beamforming algorithms associated to UL beam controlling shall be disabled for UCA cells :

  * No UL beam sweeping (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2062_replaced([11112532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWn0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * No UL beam fallback (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2041_replaced([11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * No UL Beam Probing Before DL Beam Change (5G_UP_ALG_1888_replaced([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2056_replaced([11112507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * No dynamic UL beam updating (5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

### 3.2.7.4 UL beam management for ULA cell with 1 SSB

#### 3.2.7.4.0-1 UL beam management for ULA cell with 1 SSB Beam ID specification in ULA Cell with 1 SSB for UL reception (ID: 13256670)

**3.2.7.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13256671`)

UL beam management for ULA cell with 1 SSB When Uniform Linear Array (ULA) cell is configured ([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and NRCELL.numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks=1 and NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming=4RX, 2 UL beam weights shall be required for all UL channels to configure 4RX in ULA cell.

The selected UL beams are delivered in the interface (reference to ([11288959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp-J8PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Each two consecutive eAxCs, which separately map to different polarities of RFU TRX groups, shall use the same pattern ID of beam weight.

For this 1 SSB ULAcase legacy UL beamforming algorithms associated with UL beam controlling shall be disabled: 

  * No UL beam sweeping ([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)[11112532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWn0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * No UL beam fallback ([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ),[11112416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * No UL Beam Probing Before DL Beam Change ([11111451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ),[11112507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpWnw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
  * No dynamic UL beam updating [11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))



Rationale:

When UL is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL C4 subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two half-sector beams combining into a full sector shall be used.

This applies for PUSCH and PRACH receptions.

---

#### 3.2.7.5 DL/UL beam management for Supercell

##### 3.2.7.5.0-1 DL/UL beam management for Supercell Beam ID specification in Supercell (ID: 11113064)

**3.2.7.5.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11113076`)

DL/UL beam management for Supercell A [CB009543-A] TDD [End CB009543-A] Supercell associates number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with equal number of virtual SSB beams, for UL and DL channels.

The associated virtual SSB beam IDs are mapped to L1 subcell IDs. The patternId is not provided to RU or L1.

The virtual SSB beam, SSB beam ID, is utilized in beam control algorithm.

---

### 3.2.7.6 Long PUCCH beamforming

#### 3.2.7.6.0-1 Long PUCCH beamforming TDD: Beams applicable to Long PUCCH (ID: 11113083)

**3.2.7.6.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11113103`)

Long PUCCH beamforming IF PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==True) is enabled then PUCCH Format 3 shall be received over at least 1 UE-best-reported SSB (coarse) beam, even if refined beams are available (and used for PUSCH reception).

If actLongPucchF1F3BfOnOranExtT6 is True, then PUCCH F1 and PUCCH F3 shall be received over at least 1 UE-best-reported SSB (coarse) beam, even if refined beams are available (and used for PUSCH reception), for details see 5G_UP_ALG_2218_replaced([11113106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5MvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UL_ALG_7023.

**Note. 2RX with beamforming is not supported on ABIO (not restricted in configuration!)**

If PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the number of UE-best reported SSB beams is derived based on below inequality:

IF actLongPucchF1F3BfOnOranExtT6 is True THEN

PUCCH Format 3 shall be received with two UE-reported best SSB beams, see 5G_UP_ALG_2218_replaced([11113106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5MvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

ELSEIF PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==True) THEN

**IF rrmMaxNumBeamsUlStream < **MaxNumUesFdmUl + 1 + (nActivatedSsPbch _(nActivatedSsPbch -1))/2,_ ***

THEN,

\- If PUCCH is received over 8 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2PS shall select four beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

\- Else PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PUCCH Format 3 shall be received with single UE-reported best SSB beam AND a full-sector beam.

**ELSE,**

\- The detailed requirement refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2218_replaced([11113106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpa5MvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**END**

where, if NIDD:actEcpri72e == 0, **MaxNumUesFdmUl in** IF condition shall be equal to max(rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl, 4) ; else if NIDD:actEcpri72e != 0, MaxNumUesFdmUl shall be set to 0.****

**Note. "+ 1" in the condition stands for Format 1 sector beam (or two-half sectors).**

rrmMaxNumBeamsUlStream is a Radio Unit - reported parameter defined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2526_replaced([11297475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqHT4PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), see also 5G_UP_ALG_4960_replaced([11199244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rrmMaxNumBeamsUlStream is expected to be set to 24 for 22R1 Nokia RUs, and should not be lower than 17 (for legacy radios not supporting latest eCPRI updates, refer also to CFAM of CB007731).

rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl is calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_4960_replaced([11199244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==True) THEN

PUCCH Format 1 shall be received over sector beam.

If PUCCH is received over 2 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), single full-sector beam shall be used.

If PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two half-sector beams combining into a full sector shall be used.

If actLongPucchF1F3BfOnOranExtT6 is True THEN PUCCH Format 1 shall be received over SSB beams.

If PUCCH is received over 2 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), best beam shall be used.

If PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))two SSB beams combining shall be used.

IF PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is NOT enabled (pucchF3BeamformingEnabled==False) THEN

whole Long PUCCH shall be received over sector beam (as per CB006064-D)

All alocations have the same PRB boundaries within the cell (the startPrb/numPrb are the same for the given PRB across all streams of a cell).

Enabling of Long PUCCH Format3 beamforming (CB007449-B) is a decision in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2526_replaced([11297475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqHT4PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), decided as combination of actLongPucchPhase2, RU capability and aR&D parameter from CPlane. This way, some CB007449 capabilities (e.g. capacity update) can be enabled independently of RU capability, which is prerequisite to PUCCH Format 3 beamforming.

**Note. Outcome of 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2526_replaced([11297475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqHT4PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is a separate beamforming flag pucchF3BeamformingEnabled - in order to allow enabling of actLongPucchPhase2 (e.g. the PUCCH capacity updates) even on radios that do not support extension type 12.**

Sector beam definition is provided in 5G_UP_ALG_2037_replaced([11112372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Note: If the NIDD actUlSrsBm is TRUE, there is no impact on PUCCH receiving beams agorithm. SRS based beam(s) is(are) only applied to PUSCH.**

**[CB013442-D]**

If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_32388_replaced([11113948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detail four beams for PUCCH F1 & F3.

**[End CB013442-D]**

---

#### 3.2.7.6.0-2 Long PUCCH beamforming TDD: Handling of 2 beams (4RX) or 4 beams (8RX) for PUCCH Format 3 (ID: 11113106)

**3.2.7.6.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11113124`)

Long PUCCH beamforming Whenever possible (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PUCCH Format 3 shall be received over

\- 2 UE-reported best SSB beams if PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

\- 4 best SSB beams if PUCCH is received over 8 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Regardless of UE-reported beam, only SSB (coarse) beams are used for PUCCH Format 3 reception. Ie, if the beams stored in UE context are refined beams, for PUCCH Format 3, the corresponding SSBs shall be used.

When UE reports only 1 beam instead of 2 (nrOfReportedRS = n1 in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2684_replaced([11303281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqj_0PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR IF the best SSB beam is same as the second best SSB beam, then:

\- For two beams (PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), the second best SSB beam shall be changed to a random neighboring SSB beam to ensure two beams are always different.

\- For four beams (PUCCH is received over 8 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), L2RT shall select four beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: If UE report two beams AND the best SSB beam is different from the second best SSB beam, L2RT shall also find four beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if PUCCH is received over 8 spatial streams.

If PUCCH is received over 4 spatial streams, L2-PS shall apply specific order of the two best beams (also after beam change) to PUCCH, so that SSB with lower ID is assigned to 1st Xpol and SSB with the highest ID is assigned to the last Xpol.

If PUCCH is received over 8 spatial streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the order of SSB beam assigned to each Xpol for PUCCH shall refer to 5G_UP_ALG_21306_replaced([11113376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: For Long PUCCH, beam sweeping is disabled: appliedUlBeamSweeping is set to FALSE (see PR636997).

For two beams if PUCCH is received over 4 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

  * IF the 2nd beam used for PUCCH Format 3 reception is the full-sector beam, the SSB is assigned to the 1st Xpol, and the full-sector beam is applied to the 2nd Xpol.



Note when actLongPucchF1F3BfOnOranExtT6 is True the 2nd beam used cannot be represented by full-sector beam.

For four beams if PUCCH is received over 8 streams (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

-If half-sector beams are used for PUCCH Format 3 reception, the 1st SSB beam is assigned to the 1st Xpol, the SSB beam which has the highest correlation with the 1st SSB beam is assigned to the 2nd Xpol and the half-sector beams are applied to the 3rd and 4th Xpol.

Rationale: For Xpol-0 & Xpol1 (4RX), the pair of SSB beams A-B or B-A are considered different beams from the Radio Unit perspective. Due to Radio Unit limitation of beams per symbol, L2PS shall consider to protect this amount by proper beam-to-Xpol ordering (so that always only A-B combinations are sent to the RU). E.g. for 6 SSBs beamset, this allows for usage of 15 instead of 30 beam combinations, with a typical Radio Unit limitation of 32 beams/symbol. For details, see also CFAM of CB007731.

L2PS shall track the assigned beam combinations, and group allocations using the same SSB beams pair under the same regionId/eCpriSectionId, as described in 5G_UP_ALG_5163_replaced([11204341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013442-D]

If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_32388_replaced([11113948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detail four beams for PUCCH F3.

[End CB013442-D]

---

#### 3.2.7.6.0-3 Long PUCCH beamforming TDD: Handling of 2 beams (4RX) for PUCCH Format 1 (ID: 11113127)

**3.2.7.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11113132`)

Long PUCCH beamforming Whenever possible (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PUCCH Format 1 shall be received over 2 UE-reported best SSB beams.

Regardless of UE-reported beam, only SSB (coarse) beams are used for PUCCH Format 1 reception. Ie, if the beams stored in UE context are refined beams, for PUCCH Format 1, the corresponding SSBs shall be used.

When UE reports only 1 beam instead of 2 (nrOfReportedRS = n1 in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2684_replaced([11303281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqj_0PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR IF the best SSB beam is same as the second best SSB beam, then the second best SSB beam shall be changed to a random neighboring SSB beam to ensure two beams are always different.

L2-PS shall apply specific order of the two best beams (also after beam change) to PUCCH, so that SSB with lower ID is assigned to 1st Xpol, and SSB with higher ID is assigned to the 2nd Xpol.

Rationale: For Xpol-0 & Xpol1 (4RX), the pair of SSB beams A-B or B-A are considered different beams from the Radio Unit perspective. Due to Radio Unit limitation of beams per symbol, L2PS shall consider to protect this amount by proper beam-to-Xpol ordering (so that always only A-B combinations are sent to the RU). E.g. for 6 SSBs beamset, this allows for usage of 15 instead of 30 beam combinations, with a typical Radio Unit limitation of 32 beams/symbol. For details, see also CFAM of CB007731.

L2PS shall track the assigned beam combinations, and group allocations using the same SSB beams pair under the same regionId/eCpriSectionId, as described in 5G_UP_ALG_5163_replaced([11204341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.2.7.6.0-4 Long PUCCH beamforming FDD: Beams applicable to long PUCCH (ID: 12770624)

**3.2.7.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12770626`)

Long PUCCH beamforming If the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): fixed beamSet#4 for UL ([12704402: Dynamic SSB/Refined beam generation for beam weights](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LsQRwWB_EfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be indicated both PUCCH F3 and F1.

---

### 3.2.7.8 PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported

### 3.2.7.8-1 PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported

#### 3.2.7.8-1.0-2 PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported If NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true and massive MIMO power saving indicator received from CPRT, 5G-L2-PS shall use the corresponding power saving beams for DL scheduling. If NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true) and (massive MIMO non-power saving indicator received from CPRT, 5G-L2-PS shall use the corresponding legacy beams for DL scheduling. [CB012170-A] [Before PR810911] If NRBTS.actSSBBoostInmMIMOMuting is true while cell is in power saving mode, legacy beams rather than power saving beams shall be used for SSB. If NRBTS.actSSBBoostInmMIMOMuting is false while cell is in power saving mode, power saving beams shall be used for SSB. [PR810911] If NRBTS.actSSBBoostInmMIMOMuting is TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall use the proper SSB beam (legacy or power saving beam) according to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16835_replaced( 11318715 ). [End PR810911] Please refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2475_replaced( 11288953 ) for the configurations of legacy and power saving beams. [End CB012170-A] Note 1: 5G-L2-PS shall not use legacy beams (even hardcoded beam) for DL scheduling any more while cell is in power saving mode [CB012170-A]and NRBTS.actSSBBoostInmMIMOMuting is False [End CB012170-A], corresponding power saving beams shall be applied instead. Note 2 : 5G-L2-PS shall use the corresponding legacy beams for UL scheduling always no matter cell is in power saving mode or not. (ID: 11113372)

2) If the number of refinement beams stored in UE context is one, L2RT shall map this refinement beam to the corresponding SSB beam and select four refinement beams in the same SSB beam envelope as the final four beams.

4) If the number of SSB beams stored in UE contest is two, L2RT shall find two correlated refinement beams for each SSB beam. According to the simulation results, the correlate refinement beams for different SSB beam shall not be duplicated.

#### 3.2.7.8-2.0-3 PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported Extend one SSB beam to four beams (8RX) (ID: 11113585)

**3.2.7.8-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12712327`)

PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported If rdOneBeamExtension(5G_UP_ALG_26328_replaced([11114150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to 0:

\- For normal UL traffic, L2RT shall find four refinement beams included in the same SSB beam stored in UE context;

\- For MSG3, L2RT shall find four beams as the combination of best SSB beam in UE context + correlated SSB beam + two half sector beams

Else if rdOneBeamExtension(5G_UP_ALG_26328_replaced([11114150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to 1:

\- For both of MSG3 and normal UL traffic, L2RT shall find four refinement beams included in the same SSB beam stored in UE context.

End

[PR842024] Note: If NIDD:basicBeamSet is configured as beamSet_2, to avoid duplicated beams on PUSCH, L2RT shall always find two high correlated refinement beams from each SSB beam in beamSet_2, regardless of the configuration of rdOneBeamExtension ([11114150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This rule applies to both normal uplink traffic and MSG3, and is consistent with the algorithm defined in algorithm [11112346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpVZofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End PR842024]

---

#### 3.2.7.8-2.0-4 PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported Extend SSB beams for PUSCH (16RX) (ID: 11113592)

**3.2.7.8-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11113598`)

PatternIDs for CSI-RS while SSB based Beam supported If NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 16 AND rdSuUeReceiverSize(5G_UP_ALG_27595_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 16:

\- If two [CB010708-I] different [End CB010708-I] SSB beams are stored in UE context, L2PS shall select four refinement beams in the same SSB beam envelope and construct 8 beams. 16RX IRC receiver shall be used.

\- If only one SSB beam [CB010708-I] or two same [End CB010708-I] SSB beams are stored in UE context, beam selection refer to 5G_UP_ALG_26331_replaced([11113585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 8RX IRC receiver shall be used.

Note, The same rule shall be applied to all of beam sets in this case.

If NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 16 AND rdSuUeReceiverSize(5G_UP_ALG_27595_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 8:

\- L2RT shall select 4 beams according to 5G_UP_ALG_26331_replaced([11113585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_22566_replaced([11113416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpbgUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 8RX IRC receiver shall be used.

5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001] is 6, L2 PS shall obtain the SSB beam IDs and correspoding patternIds as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_11982_replaced([11111700](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during cell setup. Additional, L2 PS shall obtain the ssbGroupForSsbBasedBF (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_6624_replaced([11299404](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqThIPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For each SSB group, that is firstSsbGroup, secondSsbGroup, thirdSsbGroup and fourthSsbGroup, contained in ssbGroupForSsbBasedBF, there are four SSB beams are masked as bit “1”. Below is the example of fourthSsbGroup. L2 PS shall save the information of SSB groups configurations.

[image-0][image_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating a concept related to "fourthSsbGroup". On the left, the text "fourthSsbGroup" is present. To the right of this text, a rectangular box contains the binary string "0b00101101". Four blue arrows originate from different positions within this binary string and point downwards towards four labels: "SSB Beam ID 5", "SSB Beam ID 3", "SSB Beam ID 2", and "SSB Beam ID 0". The arrow pointing to "SSB Beam ID 5" originates from the first '0' in the binary string. The arrow pointing to "SSB Beam ID 3" originates from the second '0'. The arrow pointing to "SSB Beam ID 2" originates from the third '1'. The arrow pointing to "SSB Beam ID 0" originates from the last '1'. The labels are arranged below the binary string, with "SSB Beam ID 5" and "SSB Beam ID 2" on the top row, and "SSB Beam ID 3" and "SSB Beam ID 0" on the bottom row, slightly offset.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_4989.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

For each SSB groups, L2PS can get beam index for each SSB beam ID according to bit value in SSB group. As above example of fourthSsbGroup, beam index 0 is SSB beam ID 0, beam index 1 is SSB beam ID 2, beam index 2 is SSB beam ID 3 and beam index 3 is SSB beam ID 5.

4 SSB beams in each SSB groups shall be used for one row 8 CSI-RS transmission. 4 patternId of those 4 beams shall be arranged as below:

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains a table with three columns: "CSI-RS port", and "SSB beam ID". The first column lists "1st symbol" and "2nd symbol". The second column lists CSI-RS port numbers: 3000, 3001, 3004, and 3005. The third column describes the mapping of SSB beam IDs to beam indexes.

Symbol | CSI-RS port | SSB beam ID  
---|---|---  
1st symbol | 3000 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 0  
1st symbol | 3001 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 2  
1st symbol | 3004 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 0  
1st symbol | 3005 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 2  
2nd symbol | 3000 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 1  
2nd symbol | 3001 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 3  
2nd symbol | 3004 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 1  
2nd symbol | 3005 | SSB beam ID maps to beam index 3

## 3.2.8 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management

### 3.2.8.0-1 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management UE capabilities for beamforming function (ID: 13479285)

**3.2.8.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13479271`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management **NOTE: The 'UE capabilities for beamforming' (FGCR-3077) introduces following function.**

**[Before CB013712-B]**

In FR2 only:

  * In C-Plane only: UE capability check: max. number of TRS per CC. _csi-RS-ForTracking.maxConfiguredResourceSetsPerCC [38.306, §4.2], which indicates the maximum number of TRS resource sets configured to UE per CC. It is mandated to report at least 8 for FR1 and 16 for FR2. That is FG#2-51-3. [38.822, §4.1]._
  * In C-Plane only: UE capability check: _csi-RS-ForTracking.maxConfiguredResourceSetsAllCC_[38.306, §4.2], which indicates the maximum number of TRS resource sets configured to UE across CCs. The UE is mandated to report at least 16 for FR1 and 32 for FR2. That is FG#2-51-4. [38.822, §4.1].**
  * Impact to U-Plane: RRC re-configuring supported number TRS per CC and overall CCs, enabling CA support w/ 8 CCs. UE supported number of TRS resource sets per CC is signalled by C-plane in _beamGroupSize in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._



**[End CB013712-B]**

In FR1 & FR2:

  * Impact to U-Plane: Optionally configurable, RRC re-configure RLM/BFD _failureDetectionResources to target SSB for every beam change. Assuming current default configuration depends on the UE capability_ csi-RS-RLM [38.306,§4.2]. That is FG#1-7 [38.802, §4.1]. That is indicated (MRBTS.NRBTS.NRCELL.actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch).**
  * Impact to U-Plane: UE capability check: _maxNumberNonGroupBeamReporting [38.306, §4.2], which defines support of non-group based RSRP reporting using N_max RSRP values reported. That is FG#2-29 [38.822, §4.1]. UE supported number of reported best beams is provided by C-Plane in_ nrOfReportedRS in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2684_replaced([11303281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tqj_0PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

### 3.2.8.0-3 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Initial beamGroup selection for FR2 SA (ID: 11113612)

**3.2.8.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13477683`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management For FR2 SA, during Random Access procedure when RA-Msg3 PDU contains a UL-CCCH SRB0 (5G_UP_ALG_18165_replaced([11152892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksierPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-RT shall select the initial beam group (5G_UP_ALG_10600_replaced([11113722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on beamGroupSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) received from CP-RT.

This initial beam group shall contain the initial SSB beam which was used during Random Access.

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = false the inital beam group containing initial beam shall be reported in the User Setup Response to CP-RT.

Once the UE capability is known, if L2-RT received the updated beamGroupSize value from CP-RT during the User Modify procedure, it shall select the beam group according to the newly received beamGroupSize.

[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

### 3.2.8.0-4 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management RRC Reconfiguration for Beam Switch (actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch) disabled (ID: 11113619)

**3.2.8.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11113623`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = FALSE and if the inital beam group is defined during (or just after) initial access, 5G_UP_ALG_2227_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2-PS shall send it in BeamGroupChangeInd.beamGroup with invalid targetSsbBeam to C-Plane, for analog beamforming (rrmBeamformingType = analogBf, 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = FALSE and if analog beamforming (rrmBeamformingType = analogBf, 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall send beamGroupChangeInd message 5G_UP_ALG_2233_replaced([11113759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8gvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) at each beam change, only if the active beamGroup 5G_UP_ALG_2227_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) does not include the 1st target beam 5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced([11112105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In the message beamGroupChangeInd, the vector beamGroup shall include SSB-Indices as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2227_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the parameter targetSsbBeam should be invalid.

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = FALSE and if digital beamforming (rrmBeamformingType = digitalBf, 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 'UE capabilities for beamforming' (FGCR-3077) is not applicable and L2-PS shall not sent beamGroupChangeInd.

*beamFormingType introduce in Identify the RU beamforming capability, where OAM reads the RU beaforming capability, and sends it to CP-RT via CpRtCm_CellMappingReq, and then CP-RT sends it to L2RT via this IE

### 3.2.8.0-6 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Consecutive Beam failure recovery handling (ID: 13446317)

**3.2.8.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13446320`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Upon reception of RACH message 3 due to a BFR (Msg3 received with CRNTI in [11152921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksjFsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB should evaluate if this RACH procedure follows another RACH procedure from BFR with not successful reception of UL messages for the UE.

In such cases, gNB should trigger the reconfiguration of the UE SRS, CSI and PUCCH resources before scheduling any traffic.

### 3.2.8.0-7 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management RRC Reconfiguration for Beam Switch (actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch) enabled (ID: 11113629)

**3.2.8.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11113636`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE and if the initial target beam is defined during or after initial access, 5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2-PS shall send it in BeamGroupChangeInd.targetSsbBeam with empty beamGroup to C-Plane, if NSA user for SgNB addition (5G_CP_DC_62_replaced([10955345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-Jo_Z_u3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_282_replaced([10956546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-J3o5fu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_954_replaced([10958448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-KZNXfu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_1188_replaced([10959490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-KmBoPu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_1560_replaced([10961118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-K6KvPu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) related procedures. If SA user for Initial Access (5G_CP_OTH_1198_replaced([11612017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y5Sb1vwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_OTH_1517_replaced([11615732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y544svwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) related procedures, L2-PS shall send this targetSsbBeam in PsUser_UserSetpResp message to C-Plane.

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE, L2-PS shall send beamGroupChangeInd (5G_UP_ALG_2233_replaced([11113759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8gvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at each beam change 5G_UP_ALG_2006_replaced([11112105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with a targetSsbBeam = 1st target beam as in 5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and empty beamGroup, for Beamforming mode (see 5G_UP_ALG_2183_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_907_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE: If beamGroupSize value (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) is equal to [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] (NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks) [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001], only RLM/BFD failureDetectionResources are RRC re-configure to the target SSB beam. That is always in FR1. If beamGroupSize value (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) is smaller than [Before CB008285-E-UPD001] NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks [CB008285-E-UPD001] number of activated SS/PBCH (nActivatedSsPbch, see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008285-E-UPD001], RLM/BFD failureDetectionResources and only one TRS resource set are RRC re-configure to the target SSB beam.

[Before CB008285-E-UPD001]

If beamGroupSize = numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks , beam change shall be signalled by MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication for Coreset#N, where N !=0 and usually N = 1.

If beamGroupSize < numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks , this MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication shall not be sent, and instead RRC re-configuration of CoreSet#N shall be assumed, see also message sequence chart in 5G_UP_ALG_2233_replaced([11113759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8gvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_1093_replaced([11354989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucM8zPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If beamGroupSize < numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks , and if the target beam is defined by the Beam Failure Procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication shall be sent after completed RRC re-configuration of CoreSet#N , according to 5G_UP_ALG_3439_replaced([11152968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksjFufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008285-E-UPD001]

[CB008285-E-UPD001]

If beamGroupSize = nActivatedSsPbch, beam change shall be signalled by MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication for Coreset#N, where N !=0 and usually N = 1.

If beamGroupSize < nActivatedSsPbch, this MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication shall not be sent, and instead RRC re-configuration of CoreSet#N shall be assumed, see also message sequence chart in 5G_UP_ALG_2233_replaced([11113759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8gvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_1093_replaced([11354989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucM8zPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If beamGroupSize < nActivatedSsPbch, and if the target beam is defined by the Beam Failure Procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication shall be sent after completed RRC re-configuration of CoreSet#N , according to 5G_UP_ALG_3439_replaced([11152968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksjFufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: nActivatedSsPbch is the number of activated SS/PBCH (see 5G_UP_82_replaced([11347116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJz2PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008285-E-UPD001]

### 3.2.8.0-8 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management [Before CNI-107035] beamGroupChangeAck = FALSE [CNI-107035] gNB internal procedure failure [End CNI-107035] (ID: 11113639)

**3.2.8.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `11113649`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management [CNI-107035] Refactored by CNI-107035. [End CNI-107035]

If the reconfiguration enter gNB internal failure, 5G-L2-PS shall:

trigger the rrc reconfiguration procedure again with the same beam group. The same beam group shall only be sent per UE two times consecutively.

### 3.2.8.0-9 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management BeamGroup in the UE context (ID: 11113653)

**3.2.8.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11113663`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management If PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is received, L2-PS shall update the active beamGroup of a UE. If target beam (as in 5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) was not included in the previous beamGroup and is included in the updated active beamGroup, then L2-PS shall send the pending MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication as in 5G_UP_ALG_2104_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), if beamGroupSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 1.

If actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE and beamGroupSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = 1, L2-PS shall straightly schedule in DL and UL by sending DCI and shall not sent MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication.

NOTE: Coreset#0 is assumed to be on target beam by C-Plane RRC re-configuration.

The beamGroupSize of a UE shall be defined by the value of UserSetup.pdschConfig.beamGroupSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE: The value of beamGroupSize shall be set = 1, if analog beamforming (rrmBeamformingType = analogBf, 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and MRBTS.NRBTS.NRCELL.actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE.

If actORuFlexibleBeamGrpMapping = false, then the beam group definition and the mapping of an initial beam to an initial beamGroup are as 5G_UP_ALG_10595_replaced([11113685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_10595_replaced([11113685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_10600_replaced([11113722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_10604_replaced([11113749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

BeamGroupChangeInd.beamGroup shall only be used if beamGroupSize is set != {1, N}, where N is the full number of SSB beams. If the beamGroupSize = 16, the beamGroups are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10595_replaced([11113685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the mapping of an initial beam to an initial beamGroup of a UE is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10600_replaced([11113722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008490-L]For NR-DC, the beam group definition and the mapping of an initial beam to an initial beamGroup are as 5G_UP_ALG_10599_replaced([11113712](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_26558_replaced([11113737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_10604_replaced([11113749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_26621_replaced([11113701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

BeamGroupChangeInd.beamGroup shall only be used if beamGroupSize is set != {1, N}, where N is the full number of SSB beams. If the beamGroupSize = 11, the beamGroups are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10599_replaced([11113712](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the mapping of an initial beam to an initial beamGroup of a UE is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26558_replaced([11113737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008490-L]

If actORuFlexibleBeamGrpMapping = true, then the beam group is configured by operator (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1952_replaced([11111852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The initial beamGroup is same as the beam group configured by operator. During or after initial access, gNB shall map the initial target beam to initial beamGroup which is the first beam group including the initial target beam.

**3.2.8.0-10.0-5**  (ID: `11113712`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Beam Groups Size = 16 or 11 and Beam Set Size = 56 for ABF

---

**3.2.8.0-10.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13477685`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management This requirement defines beam groups of size = 16 or beam groups of size = 11 for analog beamforming related beam set of size = 56. The beamGroup shall be input from NRBTS/NRCELL/NRBEAMMAP. **For NR-DC beam groups are provided by NRBTS/NRCELL/NRBEAMMAP/duBeamGrpListForNRDC.**

[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

**3.2.8.0-10.0-6**  (ID: `13356929`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Beam Groups Size greater than or equal to Beam Set Size

---

**3.2.8.0-10.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13478745`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Whenever the beam group size is greater than or equal to the size of the beamset the single beam group containing all beams of the beamset shall be applied.

In the example of beamSetAbf_32A, initial beamIds {0-5, 16-20} are mapped to beamGroup#0, initial beamIds {6-9, 21-25, 31} are mapped to beamGroup#1, and initial beamIds {10-15, 26-30} are mapped to beamGroup#2, as beam sets are defined in 5G_L2_478_replaced([11155875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248IMfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the example of beamSetAbf_32B, & beamSetAbf_32C, initial beamIds {0-3, 11-13, 21-24} are mapped to beamGroup#0, initial beamIds {4-6, 14-17, 25-27} are mapped to beamGroup#1, and initial beamIds {7-10, 18-20, 28-31} are mapped to beamGroup#2, as beam sets are defined in 5G_UP_ALG_1902_replaced([11111481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The above mapping shall define the new beam group if the target beam is not inlcuded the current beam group.

The above mapping shall define the new beam group if the target beam is not inlcuded in the current beam group.

**3.2.8.0-11.0-5**  (ID: `11113749`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management **Beam Group Size =11 or 16 and Beam Sets of Size = 56 for ABF**

---

**3.2.8.0-11.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13478824`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management The initial beam group and the included Beam Ids (which are the SSBRI values) are defined by the initial SSB-Index from the RACH procedure as in 5G_UP_ALG_3388_replaced([11152417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the configured beam set from MRBTS.NRBTS.NRCELL.beamSet, as defined in this requirement.

Rationale: for intial beam group mapping, there should be no overlaping between different groups, otherwise it will lead to ambiguity for which group this UE belongs.

The group is defined as removing the overlapped the beams between adjacient groups defined in for beam groups of size 16 defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10595_replaced([11113685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or for beam groups of size 11 in NR-DC defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26621_replaced([11113701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

---

**3.2.8.0-11.0-6**  (ID: `13356938`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Beam Groups Size greater than or equal to Beam Set Size

---

**3.2.8.0-11.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13478848`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Whenever the initial beam group size is greater than or equal to the size of the beamset the single beam group containing all beams of the beamset shall be applied.

[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

Indication Success Case NOTE: version 2019-12-12 [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between a 5G UE (User Equipment) and a gNB-DU (next-generation NodeB - Distributed Unit). The gNB-DU is further divided into two components: 5G-L2-PS and 5G-CP-RT. The diagram depicts two alternative scenarios, indicated by the "Alt" keyword. **Scenario 1 (beamGroup Size > 1):** 1\. The 5G UE sends a "MAC_CE_PDCCH_TCI-State_Ind(CS-1)" message to the gNB-DU, with a reference to "(5G_RAN_UP_15888)". 2\. The gNB-DU responds with a "DCI DL/UL Allocation on target beam". **Scenario 2 (beamGroup Size = 1):** 1\. The gNB-DU sends a "DCI DL/UL Allocation on target beam" to the 5G UE. 2\. The 5G UE then sends "DL/UL data on target beam" to the gNB-DU. The diagram shows that the decision point for these two scenarios is based on the "beamGroup Size".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_5046.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] File: FGCR-3077_beamGroupChange_successful.png Folder: Chart references: (1) NOTE: MAC CE for CoreSet(CS)#1 is sent on source beam if before Beam Failure Recovery. MAC CE is sent on target beam if after Beam Failure Recovery. For Inital BeamGroupChangeInd message, MAC CE is not sent after having received RrcReconfCompleteReq since the serving beam Id is the target beam Id, if NSA user for SgNB addition (5G_CP_DC_62_replaced([10955345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-Jo_Z_u3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_282_replaced([10956546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-J3o5fu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_954_replaced([10958448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-KZNXfu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_1188_replaced([10959490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-KmBoPu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_DC_1560_replaced([10961118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-K6KvPu3Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) related procedures. (2) See 5G_UP_ALG_2225_replaced([11113629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_2223_replaced([11113619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). NOTE: If beamGroupSize (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2643_replaced([11302387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfuZPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 1, after Beam Failure Procedure, MAC CE PDCCH TCI State Indication shall be sent after completed RRC re-configuration of CoreSet#N, see 5G_UP_ALG_2225_replaced([11113629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). NOTE: On CP3 level, TTI logs and counters shall be be defined logging or counting the event of the messages BeamGroupChangeInd, UserModifyReq, and RrcReconfCompleteReq. .[End CNI-107035]

Management 11113785: Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management 11113785: Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management [Before CNI-107035]Message Sequence Chart: Beam Group Change Indication Failure Case

NOTE: version 2019-12-12

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between a 5G UE (User Equipment) and a gNB-DU (Next Generation NodeB - Distributed Unit). The diagram depicts various messages and events exchanged between these entities, along with conditional logic and timers. Here's a breakdown of the elements: **Participants:** * **5G UE:** Represents the user equipment. * **gNB-DU:** Represents the distributed unit of the next-generation base station. * **5G-L2-PS:** Likely refers to Layer 2 Protocol Stack within the gNB-DU. * **5G-CP-RT:** Likely refers to Control Plane - Real-Time component within the gNB-DU. * **Timer:** A timer component within the gNB-DU. **Sequence of Events and Messages:** 1\. **(3) At:** This indicates a point in time or a trigger for the subsequent actions. 2\. **PsUser_UserModifyReq(beamGroupChangeAck):** A request message sent from the gNB-DU to the 5G UE. 3\. **(4) Opt:** This signifies an optional path or condition. 4\. **beamGroupChangeAck == FALSE (5G_RAN_UP_24483):** A condition where the beam group change acknowledgment is false, possibly related to a specific RAN UP (Radio Access Network User Plane) message. 5\. **start beamGroupResentTimer:** The gNB-DU starts a timer named "beamGroupResentTimer". 6\. **beamGroupResentTimer timeout:** The "beamGroupResentTimer" expires. 7\. **(5) PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd:** An indication message sent from the gNB-DU to the 5G UE. 8\. **PsUser_UserModifyReq(beamGroupChangeAck):** Another request message from the gNB-DU to the 5G UE. 9\. **PsUser_RrcReconfCompleteReq:** A request message related to RRC (Radio Resource Control) reconfiguration completion. **Conditional Logic (Alt):** The diagram shows an "Alt" (Alternative) block, indicating that one of the following conditions will be met: * **received RrcReconfCompleteReq message (5G_RAN_UP_24491):** The 5G UE receives an RRC Reconfiguration Complete message. * **Alt Block 1:** * **(1) MAC_CE_PDCCH_TCI-State_Ind(CS-1):** A MAC Control Element (CE) message related to PDCCH (Physical Downlink Control Channel) TCI (Transmit Power Control Indicator) state indication. * **DCI DL/UL Allocation on target beam:** Downlink/Uplink DCI (Downlink Control Information) allocation on a target beam. * **Alt Block 2:** * **(2) beamGroup Size > 1:** A condition where the beam group size is greater than 1. * **DCI DL/UL Allocation on target beam:** Downlink/Uplink DCI allocation on a target beam. * **Alt Block 3:** * **(2) beamGroup Size = 1:** A condition where the beam group size is equal to 1. * **DCI DL/UL Allocation on target beam:** Downlink/Uplink DCI allocation on a target beam. * **DL/UL data on target beam:** Indicates the transmission or reception of Downlink/Uplink data on the target beam. * **NOT received rrcReconfCompleteReq:** The RRC Reconfiguration Complete message is not received. * **NSA: UE is RRC released, SA: UE is moved to NR idle state:** This indicates the state of the UE: * **NSA (Non-Standalone):** The UE is released from RRC connection. * **SA (Standalone):** The UE is moved to an NR (New Radio) idle state.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_5049.001.png[/image_path][/image-0].[End CNI-107035]

### 3.2.8.0-14 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Concurrent Beam Group Change (ID: 11113790)

**3.2.8.0-14.0-2**  (ID: `11113797`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management [Before CNI-107035]Concurrent Beam Group Change

If a BeamGroupChangeInd message is sent by L2-PS for a given UE, and if corresponding rrcReconfCompleteReq message has not been received, another beamGroupChangeInd message shall not be sent.

NOTE: the beam change handling via RRC re-configuration is sequential. A new beam (group) change shall only be sent by BeamGroupChangeInd if the old one was completed by rrcReconfCompleteReq message. The reason is that RRC re-configuration handling in C-Plane where any second RRC reconfiguration is dropped before the ongoing is completed. If RRC reconfiguration fails, the UE is RRC released in (NSA) or moved to idle state (SA).

If rrcReconfCompleteReq message is received, L2-PS shall send a PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message, if applicable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2223_replaced([11113619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_2223_replaced([11113619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CNI-107035]

---

### 3.2.8.0-15 Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management Beam group update during SCell addition for FR2 SA CA (ID: 11113799)

**3.2.8.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `13478988`)

Details of UE Capability Impact on Beam Management When a new beam group size is received during the user modify procedure for SCell addition, 5G L2-PS shall:

  * decide the new beam group according to the new beam group size, current best beam and the beam group defined in 5G_UP_ALG_10595_replaced([11113685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_10599_replaced([11113712](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpdVdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * Include the new beam group into user modify response message and send the response message to C-Plane.



[CB013712-B] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-B]

## 3.2.9 Beam muting

### 3.2.9.0-1 Beam muting Retrieving indices of muted beams and corresponding SSB opportunities (ID: 11113810)

**3.2.9.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13478987`)

Beam muting L2-PS shall retrieve indices of muted beams and corresponding SSB opportunities in the cell from the cell setup or during online modification received from CP.

**Note1:**

For details of the IE and its interpretation see definition of the

NRBTS/NRCELL/beamSet.beamsMuted.

**Note 2:**

SSB opportunities (i.e. absolute SSB indices in burst) which corresponds to muted beams are function of the indices of the muted beams as provided by beamsMuted and SSB positions in cell as provided by ssbPositionInBurst. Muted beam index k being set in the beamsMuted corresponds to (k+1)-th opportunity of SSB in the currently active set of SSBs as provided by ssbPositionInBurst. I.e. in terms of absolute SSB opportunities numbering for given numerology as defined in 3GPP.

[Before CB013712-B] If numOfSsBlocks is set to 56, the location of SSB blocks please refer to

[11111484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). 11 SSB blocks of 56 SSB blocks will be muted accroding to NRBTS/NRCELL/beamSet.beamsMuted to get 45 SSB blocks.[End CB013712-B]

---

### 3.2.9.0-2 Beam muting Muted beams identification (ID: 11113816)

**3.2.9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11113820`)

Beam muting L2-PS shall consider beam as muted in downlink in the cell if beam is marked as muted in 5G_UP_ALG_2237_replaced([11113810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8j_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or beam is refined beam associated to beam marked as muted in the 5G_UP_ALG_2237_replaced([11113810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8j_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

Association between beams, refined beams and SSBs are described in 5G_UP_ALG_11982_replaced([11111700](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_1937_replaced([11111754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpP6H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
