## 3.2.10 Beam control for beam validation

### 3.2.10.0-1 Beam control for beam validation Beam validation with R&amp;D parameters (ID: 11113826)

**3.2.10.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12695799`)

Beam control for beam validation [Before CNI-137616-B]

For beam validation purpose, L2-PS shall allow to control the beam(s) for PUSCH and PDSCH with R&D parameters. The beams can be any beams introduced by 5G22R2 such as SSB/refined beam, PMI beams and osDFT beams. It needs to suppport:

  1. In UL, for 4Rx-IRC/MRC receiver, R&D parameter can specify 2 beams for PUSCH receiving; These 2 beams can be same or different.

  2. In DL, R&D parameters can specify 2 beams for PDSCH sending. These 2 beams can be same or different;

  3. The beam(s) controlled by R&D parameters for UL and DL shall be in dependent;

  4. The beam(s) controlled by R&D parameters for UL and DL shall be only applied to PDSCH and PUSCH. For other channels, it shall have no impact.

  5. The beam(s) can be changed online.




The R&D parameters and implementation detail are defined in CP3.

[End CNI-137616-B]

Note: R&D parameters are removed by CNI-137616.

---

### 3.2.10.0-2 Beam control for beam validation Beam Selection for 8RX (ID: 11113833)

**3.2.10.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11113837`)

Beam control for beam validation Beam Selection for PUSCH

**3.2.10.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11113842`)

Beam control for beam validation For 8RX receiver L1 validation purpose, NIDD:NRCELL.beamSet.nrBtsBeamRefinementP2 and periodic SRS shall be disabled for the UE, in this configuration:

  * 4 SSB beams which are included the configured beamSet.e.t.c beamSet_4 or beamSet_3_1 shall be used for PUSCH channel. The first two beams which sent to gNB L1 shall be the beams which follow the legacy beam selection procedure. The last two beams which sent to gNB L1 shall be the remaining beams that are left in beamSet_4 or beamSet_3_1 after excluding the first two best beams.

rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_32388_replaced([11113948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detail four beams.

## 3.2.11 UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam

### 3.2.11.0-1 UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam Determination of dominant UL beam for Positioning (ID: 11113859)

**3.2.11.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13315442`)

UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam [CB008577-E] For TDD BF: [End CB008577-E] gNB-DU shall determine the UE's dominant horizontal and vertical UL beam among the UE’s selected valid UL beams during the latest monitoring window given by _NRBTS/NRCEL- UlAoAMonitorWindow before the determination moment._

During the monitoring window given by _NRBTS/NRCEL- UlAoAMonitorWindow before the moment of UL AoA determination, gNB-DU shall determine the newest valid UL beam pair (including horizontal beam and vertical beam) of UE's PUSCH, as below:_

\- if NRCELL/actUlSrsBm = true, and if gNB-DU selected first-best DFT beam (vBest in vertical and hBest in horizontal, see 5G_UP_ALG_2173_replaced([11154691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the UE's PUSCH, gNB-DU shall record valid first-best UL DFT beam pair.

\- else if gNB-DU didn't select DFT beam, gNB-DU shall record the valid first UL SSB or refine beam for PUSCH which was stored in UE's context (see 5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 

\- Those beam direction recorded before the latest monitoring window shall be discarded.

gNB-DU shall determine UE's dominant UL beam direction (in vertical and in horizontal) with the latest record of valid UL DFT beam; **if no UL DFT beam record, gNB-DU shall determine with the latest record of UL beam. If there is no valid beam record, gNB-DU shall not determine a valid dominant UL beam.**

[CB008577-E] For FDD BF:

  * if gNB-DU selected PMI beam for the UE's PUSCH, gNB-DU shall record the full panel PMI beam.

  * else if gNB-DU selected refinement of best GoB beam of #4 for the UE's PUSCH, gNB-DU shall record valid best GoB beam of #4, not its refinement.

  * else if gNB-DU selected fixed beam #4 for the UE's PUSCH, gNB-DU shall record full panel sector beam. [End CB008577-E]




[CB014535-SR-A-UPD002] When the gNB-DU records valid beam based on UE's PUSCH, it shall record the SFN, slot, and relative imestamp measured from January 1, 1970. This recorded information shall be reported to the higher layer along with UL AoA measurement. [End CB014535-SR-A-UPD002]

---

### 3.2.11.0-2 UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam Determination of UL AoA (ID: 11113870)

**3.2.11.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13315595`)

UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam Upon calculation of UL-AoA request for NR UL E-CID measurement for a given UE (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_13187_replaced([11325007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tsq4p_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall derive the UE's horizontal and vertical UL AoA measurement respectively by looking up the corresponding angle of arrival mapping to the determined vertical dominant beam and horizontal dominant beam (see 5G_UP_ALG_25323_replaced([11113859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpejnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Where

\- The mapping relation between the angle of arrival and the UL DFT beam ID is given by 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_5955_replaced([11296085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqFesPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * **The mapping relation between the angle of arrival and the SSB and refine beam ID is given by 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_13407_replaced([11289390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp__MvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

  * **_*[CB008577-E] The mapping relation between the angle of arrival and the PMI/internal beam set#4,#1 is given by cplane. For FDD BF, gNB-DU shall map DL and UL beam ID of the same direction._ *[End CB008577-E]******

---

### 3.2.11.0-3 UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam Determination of access point for Positioning (ID: 11113880)

**3.2.11.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11113884`)

UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam If NRBTS/NRCELL/actSupercell = true, gNB-DU shall response the latest record of valid UE's virtual SSB beam ID associated to UE's L1 subcell(see 5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when got the request from gNB-DU-CPRT (see 5G_CP_OTH_16467_replaced([11635039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y9-HcfwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 

else If NRBTS/NRCELL/numOfSubSectors >0, gNB-DU shall response the latest record of valid UE's SSB beam ID addressing UE's service sub-sector(see 5G_UP_ALG_1924_replaced([11111609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOsAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when got the request from gNB-DU-CPRT (see 5G_CP_OTH_16467_replaced([11635039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y9-HcfwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

## 3.2.12 Angle of Arrival based on DL beam

### 3.2.12.0-1 Angle of Arrival based on DL beam Determination of UE's dominant beam for Direction of Arrival (ID: 11113889)

**3.2.12.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11113892`)

Angle of Arrival based on DL beam For the sake of periodic PCMD measurement reports, gNB-DU shall determine the UE's dominant DL beam pattern for **Direction of Arrival (DoA) tracing purpose with the current valid beam used for PDSCH transmission:**

 gNB-DU shall record the valid first beam (in horizontal and vertical) for PDSCH which was stored in UE's context (see 5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), including following information of the beam

o the first beam pattern ID

o the beam type indication (in below Enum value) according to selected beam :

 2D-DFT non-tapered (see 5G_UP_ALG_6998_replaced([11156071](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9WfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 2D-DFT tapered (see 5G_UP_ALG_6998_replaced([11156071](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9WfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 

 SSB (see 5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 Refined (see 5G_UP_ALG_2018_replaced([11112156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpTkdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 PMI (see 5G_UP_ALG_2188_replaced([11112763](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEDPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 If two beams are applied for a given user(see 5G_UP_ALG_2032_replaced([11112298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUymPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall also record the valid second beam (in horizontal and vertical), including following information

o the second beam pattern ID .

 gNB-DU shall record the usage time which was counted starting from the moment of use of all beams scheduled to UE (i.e. the beam group).

---

## 3.2.13 FDD Supercell management

### 3.2.13.0-1 FDD Supercell management Subcell mapping for reporting (ID: 11113898)

**3.2.13.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11113901`)

FDD Supercell management For reporting purposes, FDD supercell mode shall reuse existing beamforming related counters by mapping Beam ID to the L1 UL subcells in an ascending order starting from Beam ID 0. This mapping shall be used for reporting purposes only and shall be used in both DL and UL.

**[CB009543-C1]**

In a similar fashion, each subcell shall be mapped to a single EIRP segment, starting from EIRP segment 1. EIRP measurement shall be handled per subcell by associating each subcell to a virtual SSB beam as indicated in 5G_UP_ALG_28182_replaced([11118904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1s_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

All DL messages are duplicated, thus it is expected that the EIRP measured in each segment is proportional to _NRCELL.pMax in each subcell. This implies that when the EIRP threshold is reached in a segment, the DL resource assignment is limited in all subcells. Please note that the EIRP resource control, if it is triggered, will thus come from the subcell with the most limiting EIRP considering the EIRP budget constrained by the power reduction factor of each segment (i.e. each subcell) according to_ NRCELL.eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList.**

**[End CB009543-C1]**

---

### 3.2.13.0-2 FDD Supercell management Initial UE serving subcell (ID: 11113905)

**3.2.13.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11113909`)

FDD Supercell management In the case of a FDD supercell, PRACH is received in all L1 UL subcells and the results shall be combined to select the subcell with the best peakMetric for each UE as stated in 5G_UP_ALG_28163_replaced([11152478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgCbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The best subcell for each UE during the PRACH shall be selected as the initial subcell for this UE for the purpose of the FDD supercell UL scheduling.

The gNB shall wait for the first SINR measurement report for a UE before setting the initial SINR value for the serving subcell and non serving subcells.

---

### 3.2.13.0-3 FDD Supercell management Measurements collection (ID: 11113912)

**3.2.13.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11113915`)

FDD Supercell management In the case of a FDD supercell, the gNB shall receive PUCCH F3 for a UE on the serving subcell. However, gNB shall also measure SINR, the signal power and the noise power of the received signal on all the UL subcells of the supercell.

gNB shall use the measured SINR on each subcell and update the values in the UE context using according to the filtering in 5G_UP_ALG_28470_replaced([11113918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: The minimum value reported on a beam shall be -23dB to stay consistent with 3GPP TS 38.214. The default value of beam and the value in case of ‘out of range’ state shall be set to the same value.

---

Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management 11113924: FDD Supercell management Upon the reception of a new measurement report for a UE following the reception of a PUCCH F3 (see 5G_UP_ALG_28468_replaced([11113912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfKrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB shall filter the measurement and update the UE context using the following formula:

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a blurry, light-colored font against a white background. The equation is: SINR(u,s) = r * SINR(u,s) + (1-r) measuredSINR(u,s)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_5090.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Where:

 SINR(u,s) is the SINR of the User u on the Subcell s

 r is the filtering coefficient defined as rdSubcellMgmtSINRFilterCoefficient in 5G_UP_ALG_28476_replaced([11114163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 measuredSINR(u,s) is the measured SINR for User u on Subcell s as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_28468_replaced([11113912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfKrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.2.13.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11113934`)

FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management 11113934: FDD Supercell management Upon the reception of a new measurement report for a UE and after filtering of the received measurements according to 5G_UP_ALG_28470_replaced([11113918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpfxsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB shall evaluate if the serving subcell for a given UE shall be updated. To do so, gNB shall compare the SINR of the current serving subcell to the best SINR among the other subcell using the following formula:

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a blurry, italicized font. The expression is: SINR(u,s) > SINR(u,i) + rdSubcellSwitchSINRThreshold.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_5092.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Where:

 SINR(u,s) is the SINR of the User u on the Subcell s

 i is the index of the serving subcell for User u

 rdSubcellSwitchSINRThreshold is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_28478_replaced([11114169](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If this formula is true, gNB shall update the serving subcell of the UE from Subcell i to Subcell s. The new subcell shall be used for UL messages reception for this UE from the next slot onwards.

## 3.2.14 Internal L3 call solution for FDD mMIMO beamforming

### 3.2.14.0-1 Internal L3 call solution for FDD mMIMO beamforming FDD mMIMO beamforming configuration (ID: 11113942)

**3.2.14.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11113945`)

Internal L3 call solution for FDD mMIMO beamforming rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, CB013442-D is enabled.

---

### 3.2.14.0-2 Internal L3 call solution for FDD mMIMO beamforming FDD mMIMO beamforming PatternID (ID: 11113948)

**3.2.14.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11113952`)

Internal L3 call solution for FDD mMIMO beamforming This requirement defines the predefined Beam and Pattern IDs which is used in CB013442. Beam weights are calculated by AntMax tool.

For AVEGHA (32T32R RU), the pattern IDs shall be defined in this requirement;

|  |  |   
---|---|---|---  
**Antenna** | **DL** | **Opening angle** | **Pattern ID**  
AVEGHA | full beam | 120 | 1  
panel split beam_1 | 120 | 2 |   
panel split beam_2 | 120 | 3 |   
**UL** | **Opening angle** | **Pattern ID** |   
full beam | 120 | 4 |   
panel split beam_1 | 120 | 5 |   
panel split beam_2 | 120 | 6 |   
panel split beam_3 | 120 | 7 |   
panel split beam_4 | 120 | 8 |   
  
Static beams are applied always in CB013442-D:

 DL beam selection:

 One static full beam (Pattern ID 1) is applied for channels requiring only one beam.

 Two static panel-split beams (Pattern ID 2, 3) are applied for channels requiring two beams.

 UL beam selection:

 8Rx shall be applied for UL if rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, hence four panel split beams (pattern ID 5, 6, 7, 8) shall be applied for PUSCH, PUCCH and A-SRS for SU MIMO , one full beam (pattern ID 4) shall be applied for PRACH.

Note 2: 5G-L2-PS shall expect the cell-specific periodic CSI-RS resource configuration (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_7924_replaced([11298666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqOoofvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_16401_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, and 2 staic panel split beams (pattern ID 2, 3) shall be applied for CSI RS for channel measurement.

---

## 3.2.15 R&amp;D parameters

### 3.2.15.0-1 R&amp;D parameters rdDisableBestPmiBeamForPdcch (ID: 11113959)

**3.2.15.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13136349`)

R&D parameters [Before CNI-137616-C] Defines which beam is used for PDCCH transmission when dlMimoMode is "CL 8x4 MIMO" is true for eCPRI case. If the parameter is 0, best PMI beam is used, else the best SSB beam feedback from UE is used.

Only default value is supported

  * for the cells with small cell bandwidth on RF6.2 32/64TRX mMIMO RUs, the cell will be indicated via NIDD:RCELL/limitedBeamsPerStreamPerSlot.
  * in tdLte config0 frame structure in BWs >=20 MHz**.**



Value range: 0...1

Default value: 1

Unit: NA

Online modifiable: No

Step size: 1

Used in: 5G_UP_ALG_1984_replaced([11112043](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpSWYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CNI-137616-C]

Note: R&D parameter removed by CNI-137616.

---

### 3.2.15.0-3 R&amp;D parameters rdFddPdcchBeamType (ID: 12806247)

**3.2.15.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12806248`)

R&D parameters This parameter which kind of beam be used for PDCCH in FDD cells.

Value range: [0,1]

0: full sector beam for DL shall be used;

1: UE specific best beam shall be used, e.g. best PMI or probing beam from #4.

Default value: 0

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step size: 1

Performance impact: need field test to show impact

Used in: ([12777257: FDD: Maximum Two beams from CSI feedback](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ldAtcI1KEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

Trigger for deletion: After product released to customer and proved which option has better performance in large field.

---

### 3.2.15.0-4 R&amp;D parameters rdBeamTogglingAddPowerOffset_dB (ID: 11113972)

**3.2.15.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11113975`)

R&D parameters Offset between L1-RSRP values of active TCI state and best beam, assuming corner case that only order of 1st and 2nd beam needs to swap. It is defined by a 7-bit value in the range [-140, -44] dBm with 1dB step size.

Value range: 0..128

Default value: 0 dB

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1 dB

Specified in: 5G_UP_ALG_7972_replaced([11112714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYdAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.2.15.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11113982`)

R&D parameters The threshold for power balancedness between best and second best beam.

Value range: [1,100]

Default value: 10 (0.1)

Unit: NA

### 3.2.15.0-7 R&amp;D parameters rdDlBeamSelectTimer (ID: 11113992)

**3.2.15.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11113999`)

R&D parameters This parameter is DL beam selection timer when actDlSrsBm is true for eCPRI case.

[CB013710-A] If reduced periodic SRS processing functionality is triggered (5G_UP_543_replaced([11351277](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubsma_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only default value is considered for simplicity. Performance of non-default value is not promised. [End CB013710-A]

Default value: : 200 slot

Unit: slot

Online modifiable: No
